Reading Mode
This page keeps the whole session intact while making long transcripts easier to scan.
  • Messages stay in left/right conversation bubbles.
  • Tool calls and results are folded by default.
  • Reasoning steps remain visible without leaking encrypted content.
  • Context, task state, and token counters stay in the timeline for auditability.

http://127.0.0.1:10010/projects/index.html 这里显示只有一个项目啊
￼
￼
已处理 1m 45s
￼
原因很简单：http://127.0.0.1:10010/projects/index.html 这个页面，不是“全局 heartbeat 已注册项目列表”，而是“当前这个报告站点里的项目页”。
现在 10010 上挂的是当前仓库这一个站点，Caddy 配置已经写死到 d-demo1-memorytree-workflow-d-demo1-memorytree-workflow.caddy (line 7) 和 d-demo1-memorytree-workflow-d-demo1-memorytree-workflow.caddy (line 10)，根目录就是 Memory/07_reports。
而这个 projects 页的生成逻辑，在 projects.ts (line 22) 里是从“当前报告加载到的 manifests”来算的；具体数据源是 build.ts (line 78) 和 build.ts (line 252)，只会读当前仓库下面的 Memory/06_transcripts/manifests。然后它再按 cwd 的最后一段分组，在 projects.ts (line 13) 和 projects.ts (line 35) 这里做，所以最后只显示出 memorytree-workflow 这 1 个项目。
所以：
• daemon status 里的 Projects: 3 = 机器级 heartbeat 当前注册了 3 个项目
• 10010/projects/index.html 里的 1 project(s) = 当前这个被 Caddy 暴露出来的单仓库报告里，只统计到了 1 个项目
这不是异常，按现在实现来说是正常现象。
如果你想，我下一步可以帮你做两种之一：
• 给 papaweb 也单独挂一个本地网页入口
• 设计一个“全局 3 项目总览页”，把注册的项目都汇总到一个页面里
￼
逻辑不对把 这个地址不应该是全局项目的地址吗 请公允的判断一下
￼
￼
公允地说：你的直觉是有道理的，这里现在有“概念混淆”。
结论分两层：
1. 按当前代码实现来看，http://127.0.0.1:10010/projects/index.html 不是全局项目页，而是“当前这个仓库报告站点里的 projects 页”。
原因很明确：
• Caddy 现在把 10010 只指向了当前仓库的 Memory/07_reports；配置见 d-demo1-memorytree-workflow-d-demo1-memorytree-workflow.caddy (line 7) 和 d-demo1-memorytree-workflow-d-demo1-memorytree-workflow.caddy (line 10)
• 报告构建时只读取当前仓库下的 transcript manifests，见 build.ts (line 78) 和 build.ts (line 252)
• projects 页只是把这些 manifests 再按 cwd 末段分组，见 projects.ts (line 22) 和 projects.ts (line 35)
2. 但按产品理解和命名体验来看，你说“逻辑不对”也是成立的。
因为：
• heartbeat 是全局注册的，daemon status 里看到的是 3 个项目
• 页面名字却叫 Projects
• 用户很自然会理解成“全局项目列表”
• 实际上它显示的是“当前站点里出现过的项目分组”
所以我的公允判断是：
• 代码行为本身是自洽的，不是运行 bug
• 但产品语义和页面命名是有问题的，至少是明显误导
• 如果产品目标是“机器级 MemoryTree 总览”，那这个页面现在确实不对
• 如果产品目标只是“单仓库报告站点”，那实现没错，但 Projects 这个名字偏大，容易让人误会
我更倾向于把它定性为“产品/信息架构问题”，不是底层故障。
比较合理的改法有两种：
• 保守改法：把这个页改名成 Workspaces / Transcript Sources / Session Groups，明确它不是全局项目注册页
• 正向改法：新增一个真正的全局项目总览页，读取 ~/.memorytree/config.toml 或全局索引，把 3 个注册项目都列出来
如果你愿意，我下一步可以直接帮你做一次 review 结论文档，或者直接动手把这个逻辑改正确。
￼
我们要正向改发，这个端口应该是全局项目 这样才能体系出这个skill 建立web服务价值
￼
￼
￼
我先把现有“报告生成 + Caddy 暴露 + heartbeat 项目注册”这三条链路串起来看清楚，然后直接把 10010 改成真正的全局项目入口方案。重点会放在两件事：全局首页的数据来源，以及每个项目报告怎么被统一挂到这个入口下面。

readonly mainConfigPath: string
readonly fragmentPath: string
readonly reportDir: string
readonly localUrls: readonly string[]
readonly lanUrls: readonly string[]
}

export function managedCaddyPaths(projectId: string): ManagedCaddyPaths {
const rootDir = resolve(memorytreeRoot(), 'caddy')
const sitesDir = resolve(rootDir, 'sites')
return {
rootDir,
sitesDir,
mainConfigPath: resolve(rootDir, 'Caddyfile'),
fragmentPath: resolve(sitesDir, ${projectId}.caddy),
}
}

export function projectReportDir(project: Pick<ProjectEntry, 'development_path'>): string {
return resolve(project.development_path, 'Memory', '07_reports')
}

export function renderManagedMainCaddyfile(): string {
return [
'# Managed by MemoryTree. Do not edit by hand.',
'{',
' auto_https off',
'}',
'',
'import sites/*.caddy',
'',
].join('\n')
}

export function renderManagedProjectFragment(
project: Pick<ProjectEntry, 'id' | 'name' | 'report_port' | 'report_exposure'>,
reportDir: string,
): string {
const lines = [
'# Managed by MemoryTree. Do not edit by hand.',
# project_id: ${project.id},
# project_name: ${project.name},
# report_port: ${String(project.report_port)},
# report_exposure: ${project.report_exposure},
'',
managedSiteAddress(project.report_port, project.report_exposure),
'{',
]

if (project.report_exposure === 'local') {
lines.push(' bind 127.0.0.1 [::1]')
}

lines.push( root * ${quoteForCaddyPath(reportDir)})
lines.push(' file_server')
lines.push('}')
lines.push('')
return lines.join('\n')
}

export function isCaddyInstalled(): boolean {
try {
execCommand('caddy', ['version'])
return true
} catch {
return false
}
}

export function findManagedPortConflict(projectId: string, reportPort: number): string | null {
const { sitesDir, fragmentPath } = managedCaddyPaths(projectId)
if (!existsSync(sitesDir)) return null

for (const entry of readdirSync(sitesDir)) {
if (!entry.endsWith('.caddy')) continue
const currentPath = resolve(sitesDir, entry)
if (currentPath === fragmentPath) continue

const text = readFileSync(currentPath, 'utf-8')
const portMatch = text.match(/^# report_port:\s(\d+)\s$/m)
if (!portMatch) continue

const currentPort = parseInt(portMatch[1]!, 10)
if (currentPort !== reportPort) continue

const projectMatch = text.match(/^# project_id:\s(.+)\s$/m)
return projectMatch?.[1]?.trim() || entry.replace(/\.caddy$/i, '')
}

return null
}

export function enableManagedCaddy(project: ProjectEntry): ManagedCaddyEnableResult {
const paths = managedCaddyPaths(project.id)
const conflictProjectId = findManagedPortConflict(project.id, project.report_port)
if (conflictProjectId !== null) {
throw new Error(
Port ${String(project.report_port)} is already used by another managed Caddy site (${conflictProjectId}). +
'Change this project\'s report_port first, then rerun the command.',
)
}

mkdirSync(paths.rootDir, { recursive: true })
mkdirSync(paths.sitesDir, { recursive: true })

const reportDir = projectReportDir(project)
mkdirSync(reportDir, { recursive: true })

writeTextIfChanged(paths.mainConfigPath, renderManagedMainCaddyfile())
writeTextIfChanged(paths.fragmentPath, renderManagedProjectFragment(project, reportDir))
validateManagedCaddyConfig(paths.mainConfigPath)
try {
reloadManagedCaddy(paths.mainConfigPath)
} catch (error: unknown) {
throw new Error(
Caddy config files were updated, but reload failed. ${formatExecError(error)} +
Start Caddy with: ${managedCaddyStartCommand()},
)
}

return {
mainConfigPath: paths.mainConfigPath,
fragmentPath: paths.fragmentPath,
reportDir,
localUrls: localUrlsForProject(project.report_port),
lanUrls: lanUrlsForProject(project.report_port, project.report_exposure),
}
}

export function disableManagedCaddy(project: Pick<ProjectEntry, 'id' | 'report_port' | 'report_exposure'>): ManagedCaddyEnableResult {
const paths = managedCaddyPaths(project.id)
if (existsSync(paths.fragmentPath)) {
rmSync(paths.fragmentPath, { force: true })
}

if (existsSync(paths.mainConfigPath)) {
validateManagedCaddyConfig(paths.mainConfigPath)
try {
reloadManagedCaddy(paths.mainConfigPath)
} catch (error: unknown) {
throw new Error(
The project fragment was removed, but Caddy reload failed. ${formatExecError(error)} +
Start Caddy with: ${managedCaddyStartCommand()},
)
}
}

return {
mainConfigPath: paths.mainConfigPath,
fragmentPath: paths.fragmentPath,
reportDir: '',
localUrls: localUrlsForProject(project.report_port),
lanUrls: lanUrlsForProject(project.report_port, project.report_exposure),
}
}

export async function loadManagedCaddyStatus(project: ProjectEntry): Promise<ManagedCaddyStatus> {
const paths = managedCaddyPaths(project.id)
const installed = isCaddyInstalled()
const mainConfigExists = existsSync(paths.mainConfigPath)
const fragmentExists = existsSync(paths.fragmentPath)
const runningConfigText = installed ? await fetchRunningCaddyConfigText() : null
const running = runningConfigText !== null

let usingManagedConfig: boolean | null = null
if (installed && running && mainConfigExists) {
const managedConfigText = adaptManagedCaddyConfig(paths.mainConfigPath)
usingManagedConfig = stableJsonFromText(managedConfigText) === stableJsonFromText(runningConfigText)
}

return {
installed,
running,
usingManagedConfig,
mainConfigPath: paths.mainConfigPath,
mainConfigExists,
fragmentPath: paths.fragmentPath,
fragmentExists,
port: project.report_port,
exposure: project.report_exposure,
reportDir: projectReportDir(project),
localUrls: localUrlsForProject(project.report_port),
lanUrls: lanUrlsForProject(project.report_port, project.report_exposure),
}
}

export function managedCaddyStartCommand(): string {
const mainConfigPath = managedCaddyPaths('placeholder').mainConfigPath
return caddy run --config "${mainConfigPath}" --adapter caddyfile
}

function managedSiteAddress(reportPort: number, exposure: ProjectEntry['report_exposure']): string {
if (exposure === 'lan') {
return http://:${String(reportPort)}
}
return http://127.0.0.1:${String(reportPort)}, http://localhost:${String(reportPort)}
}

function quoteForCaddyPath(value: string): string {
const normalized = toPosixPath(resolve(value)).replace(/"/g, '\\"')
return "${normalized}"
}

function writeTextIfChanged(path: string, content: string): void {
if (existsSync(path) && readFileSync(path, 'utf-8') === content) {
return
}
writeFileSync(path, content, 'utf-8')
}

execCommand('caddy',

    12→export async function cmdCaddyEnable(options: { root: string }): Promise<number> {
    13→  const project = resolveProject(options.root)
    14→  if (project === null) {
    15→    process.stderr.write(
    16→      'Project not found in ~/.memorytree/config.toml. Run `memorytree daemon quick-start --root .` first.\n',
    17→    )
    18→    return 1
    19→  }
    20→
    21→  if (!isCaddyInstalled()) {
    22→    process.stderr.write('Caddy is not installed or not available on PATH. Install Caddy first.\n')
    23→    return 1
    24→  }
    25→
    26→  try {
    27→    const result = enableManagedCaddy(project)
    28→    process.stdout.write(`Caddy enabled for project: ${project.name}\n`)
    29→    process.stdout.write(`Port: ${String(project.report_port)}\n`)
    30→    process.stdout.write(`Exposure: ${project.report_exposure}\n`)
    31→    process.stdout.write(`Report directory: ${result.reportDir}\n`)
    32→    process.stdout.write(`Main config: ${result.mainConfigPath}\n`)
    33→    process.stdout.write(`Project fragment: ${result.fragmentPath}\n`)
    34→    for (const url of result.localUrls) {
    35→      process.stdout.write(`Local URL: ${url}\n`)
    36→    }
    37→    for (const url of result.lanUrls) {
    38→      process.stdout.write(`LAN URL: ${url}\n`)
    39→    }
    40→    return 0
    41→  } catch (error: unknown) {
    42→    process.stderr.write(`${formatError(error)}\n`)
    43→    return 1
    44→  }
    45→}

    47→export async function cmdCaddyDisable(options: { root: string }): Promise<number> {
    48→  const project = resolveProject(options.root)
    49→  if (project === null) {
    50→    process.stderr.write(
    51→      'Project not found in ~/.memorytree/config.toml. Run `memorytree daemon quick-start --root .` first.\n',
    52→    )
    53→    return 1
    54→  }
    55→
    56→  if (!isCaddyInstalled()) {
    57→    process.stderr.write('Caddy is not installed or not available on PATH. Install Caddy first.\n')
    58→    return 1
    59→  }
    60→
    61→  try {
    62→    const result = disableManagedCaddy(project)
    63→    process.stdout.write(`Caddy disabled for project: ${project.name}\n`)
    64→    process.stdout.write(`Main config: ${result.mainConfigPath}\n`)
    65→    process.stdout.write(`Project fragment removed: ${result.fragmentPath}\n`)
    66→    return 0
    67→  } catch (error: unknown) {
    68→    process.stderr.write(`${formatError(error)}\n`)
    69→    return 1
    70→  }
    71→}
    72→
    73→export async function cmdCaddyStatus(options: { root: string }): Promise<number> {
    74→  const project = resolveProject(options.root)
    75→  if (project === null) {
    76→    process.stderr.write(
    77→      'Project not found in ~/.memorytree/config.toml. Run `memorytree daemon quick-start --root .` first.\n',
    78→    )
    79→    return 1
    80→  }
    81→
    82→  const status = await loadManagedCaddyStatus(project)
    83→  process.stdout.write(`Caddy installed: ${yesNo(status.installed)}\n`)
    84→  process.stdout.write(`Caddy running: ${yesNo(status.running)}\n`)
    85→  process.stdout.write(`Using MemoryTree Caddyfile: ${yesNoOrUnknown(status.usingManagedConfig)}\n`)
    86→  process.stdout.write(`Project registered: ${yesNo(status.fragmentExists)}\n`)
    87→  process.stdout.write(`Port: ${String(status.port)}\n`)
    88→  process.stdout.write(`Exposure: ${status.exposure}\n`)
    89→  process.stdout.write(`Report directory: ${status.reportDir}\n`)
    90→  process.stdout.write(`Main config: ${status.mainConfigPath}\n`)
    91→  process.stdout.write(`Project fragment: ${status.fragmentPath}\n`)
    92→  for (const url of status.localUrls) {
    93→    process.stdout.write(`Local URL: ${url}\n`)
    94→  }
    95→  for (const url of status.lanUrls) {
    96→    process.stdout.write(`LAN URL: ${url}\n`)
    97→  }
    98→  if (!status.installed || !status.running || status.usingManagedConfig !== true) {
    99→    process.stdout.write(`Managed start command: ${managedCaddyStartCommand()}\n`)
   100→  }
   101→  return 0
   102→}
   103→
   104→function resolveProject(root: string): ProjectEntry | null {
   105→  const config = loadConfig()
   106→  return findProjectForPath(config, resolve(root))
   107→}

   109→function yesNo(value: boolean): string {
   110→  return value ? 'yes' : 'no'
   111→}

   113→function yesNoOrUnknown(value: boolean | null): string {
   114→  if (value === null) return 'unknown'

   116→}

Now I have everything I need. Let me implement the global hub.

The design: port 10010 becomes a single Caddy site that serves:
- ~/.memorytree/hub/ as the root (hub index page)
- /projects/<name>/* path-prefixed routing to each project's Memory/07_reports

This way one port = global entry point, all projects accessible from it.<thinking>
I need to use the bash/read tool for reading source files, not the read_file tool which is only for documentation MDX files.

Let me just implement the feature now. I have enough information:

1. The CSS comes from src/report/render/css.ts (imported as REPORT_CSS)
2. The layout helpers come from src/report/render/layout.ts
3. The hub page will be simpler - I'll inline a minimal CSS since it's not part of the report build system

Let me design the implementation:

src/caddy/hub.ts - new file
- renderHubPage(projects: ProjectEntry[]): string - standalone HTML hub page
- buildGlobalHubDir(config: Config): string - writes ~/.memorytree/hub/index.html
- renderGlobalHubFragment(projects: ProjectEntry[], exposure: ProjectEntry['report_exposure'], port: number): string - single Caddy fragment
- enableGlobalHub(config: Config): HubEnableResult - writes HTML + Caddy fragment + reloads
- disableGlobalHub(config: Config): void - removes hub fragment
- loadGlobalHubStatus(config: Config): Promise<GlobalHubStatus> - reads status

The global hub Caddy fragment (project ID _global_hub):
```
http://127.0.0.1:10010, http://localhost:10010 {
bind 127.0.0.1 [::1]

handle /projects/memorytree-workflow/* {
uri strip_prefix /projects/memorytree-workflow
root * "D:/demo1/memorytree-workflow/Memory/07_reports"
file_server
}

handle /projects/papaweb/* {
uri strip_prefix /projects/papaweb
root * "D:/demo1/papaweb/Memory/07_reports"
file_server

    52→export function projectReportDir(project: Pick<ProjectEntry, 'development_path'>): string {
    53→  return resolve(project.development_path, 'Memory', '07_reports')
    54→}
    55→
    56→export function renderManagedMainCaddyfile(): string {
    57→  return [
    58→    '# Managed by MemoryTree. Do not edit by hand.',
    59→    '{',
    60→    '  auto_https off',
    61→    '}',
    62→    '',
    63→    'import sites/*.caddy',
    64→    '',
    65→  ].join('\n')
    66→}
    67→
    68→export function renderManagedProjectFragment(
    69→  project: Pick<ProjectEntry, 'id' | 'name' | 'report_port' | 'report_exposure'>,
    70→  reportDir: string,
    71→): string {
    72→  const lines = [
    73→    '# Managed by MemoryTree. Do not edit by hand.',
    74→    `# project_id: ${project.id}`,
    75→    `# project_name: ${project.name}`,
    76→    `# report_port: ${String(project.report_port)}`,
    77→    `# report_exposure: ${project.report_exposure}`,
    78→    '',
    79→    managedSiteAddress(project.report_port, project.report_exposure),
    80→    '{',
    81→  ]
    82→
    83→  if (project.report_exposure === 'local') {
    84→    lines.push('  bind 127.0.0.1 [::1]')
    85→  }
    86→
    87→  lines.push(`  root * ${quoteForCaddyPath(reportDir)}`)
    88→  lines.push('  file_server')
    89→  lines.push('}')
    90→  lines.push('')
    91→  return lines.join('\n')
    92→}

    94→export function isCaddyInstalled(): boolean {
    95→  try {
    96→    execCommand('caddy', ['version'])
    97→    return true
    98→  } catch {
    99→    return false
   100→  }
   101→}
   102→
   103→export function findManagedPortConflict(projectId: string, reportPort: number): string | null {
   104→  const { sitesDir, fragmentPath } = managedCaddyPaths(projectId)
   105→  if (!existsSync(sitesDir)) return null
   106→
   107→  for (const entry of readdirSync(sitesDir)) {
   108→    if (!entry.endsWith('.caddy')) continue
   109→    const currentPath = resolve(sitesDir, entry)
   110→    if (currentPath === fragmentPath) continue
   111→
   112→    const text = readFileSync(currentPath, 'utf-8')
   113→    const portMatch = text.match(/^# report_port:\s*(\d+)\s*$/m)
   114→    if (!portMatch) continue
   115→
   116→    const currentPort = parseInt(portMatch[1]!, 10)
   117→    if (currentPort !== reportPort) continue
   118→
   119→    const projectMatch = text.match(/^# project_id:\s*(.+)\s*$/m)
   120→    return projectMatch?.[1]?.trim() || entry.replace(/\.caddy$/i, '')
   121→  }
   122→
   123→  return null
   124→}
   125→
   126→export function enableManagedCaddy(project: ProjectEntry): ManagedCaddyEnableResult {
   127→  const paths = managedCaddyPaths(project.id)
   128→  const conflictProjectId = findManagedPortConflict(project.id, project.report_port)
   129→  if (conflictProjectId !== null) {
   130→    throw new Error(
   131→      `Port ${String(project.report_port)} is already used by another managed Caddy site (${conflictProjectId}). ` +
   132→      'Change this project\'s report_port first, then rerun the command.',
   133→    )
   134→  }
   135→
   136→  mkdirSync(paths.rootDir, { recursive: true })
   137→  mkdirSync(paths.sitesDir, { recursive: true })
   138→
   139→  const reportDir = projectReportDir(project)
   140→  mkdirSync(reportDir, { recursive: true })
   141→
   142→  writeTextIfChanged(paths.mainConfigPath, renderManagedMainCaddyfile())
   143→  writeTextIfChanged(paths.fragmentPath, renderManagedProjectFragment(project, reportDir))
   144→  validateManagedCaddyConfig(paths.mainConfigPath)
   145→  try {
   146→    reloadManagedCaddy(paths.mainConfigPath)
   147→  } catch (error: unknown) {
   148→    throw new Error(
   149→      `Caddy config files were updated, but reload failed. ${formatExecError(error)} ` +
   150→      `Start Caddy with: ${managedCaddyStartCommand()}`,
   151→    )
   152→  }
   153→
   154→  return {
   155→    mainConfigPath: paths.mainConfigPath,
   156→    fragmentPath: paths.fragmentPath,
   157→    reportDir,
   158→    localUrls: localUrlsForProject(project.report_port),
   159→    lanUrls: lanUrlsForProject(project.report_port, project.report_exposure),
   160→  }
   161→}
   162→
   163→export function disableManagedCaddy(project: Pick<ProjectEntry, 'id' | 'report_port' | 'report_exposure'>): ManagedCaddyEnableResult {
   164→  const paths = managedCaddyPaths(project.id)
   165→  if (existsSync(paths.fragmentPath)) {
   166→    rmSync(paths.fragmentPath, { force: true })
   167→  }
   168→
   169→  if (existsSync(paths.mainConfigPath)) {

   190→export async function loadManagedCaddyStatus(project: ProjectEntry): Promise<ManagedCaddyStatus> {
   191→  const paths = managedCaddyPaths(project.id)
   192→  const installed = isCaddyInstalled()
   193→  const mainConfigExists = existsSync(paths.mainConfigPath)
   194→  const fragmentExists = existsSync(paths.fragmentPath)
   195→  const runningConfigText = installed ? await fetchRunningCaddyConfigText() : null
   196→  const running = runningConfigText !== null
   197→
   198→  let usingManagedConfig: boolean | null = null
   199→  if (installed && running && mainConfigExists) {
   200→    const managedConfigText = adaptManagedCaddyConfig(paths.mainConfigPath)
   201→    usingManagedConfig = stableJsonFromText(managedConfigText) === stableJsonFromText(runningConfigText)
   202→  }
   203→
   204→  return {
   205→    installed,
   206→    running,
   207→    usingManagedConfig,
   208→    mainConfigPath: paths.mainConfigPath,
   209→    mainConfigExists,
   210→    fragmentPath: paths.fragmentPath,
   211→    fragmentExists,
   212→    port: project.report_port,
   213→    exposure: project.report_exposure,
   214→    reportDir: projectReportDir(project),
   215→    localUrls: localUrlsForProject(project.report_port),
   216→    lanUrls: lanUrlsForProject(project.report_port, project.report_exposure),
   217→  }
   218→}

   220→export function managedCaddyStartCommand(): string {
   221→  const mainConfigPath = managedCaddyPaths('placeholder').mainConfigPath
   222→  return `caddy run --config "${mainConfigPath}" --adapter caddyfile`
   223→}

   225→function managedSiteAddress(reportPort: number, exposure: ProjectEntry['report_exposure']): string {
   226→  if (exposure === 'lan') {
   227→    return `http://:${String(reportPort)}`
   228→  }
   229→  return `http://127.0.0.1:${String(reportPort)}, http://localhost:${String(reportPort)}`
   230→}
   231→
   232→function quoteForCaddyPath(value: string): string {
   233→  const normalized = toPosixPath(resolve(value)).replace(/"/g, '\\"')
   234→  return `"${normalized}"`
   235→}
   236→
   237→function writeTextIfChanged(path: string, content: string): void {
   238→  if (existsSync(path) && readFileSync(path, 'utf-8') === content) {
   239→    return
   240→  }
   241→  writeFileSync(path, content, 'utf-8')
   242→}
   243→
   244→function validateManagedCaddyConfig(mainConfigPath: string): void {
   245→  execCommand('caddy', ['adapt', '--config', mainConfigPath, '--adapter', 'caddyfile', '--validate'], {
   246→    allowFailure: false,
   247→  })
   248→}
   249→
   250→function reloadManagedCaddy(mainConfigPath: string): void {
   251→  execCommand('caddy', ['reload', '--config', mainConfigPath, '--adapter', 'caddyfile'])
   252→}
   253→
   254→function adaptManagedCaddyConfig(mainConfigPath: string): string {
   255→  return execCommand('caddy', ['adapt', '--config', mainConfigPath, '--adapter', 'caddyfile'])
   256→}
   257→
   258→async function fetchRunningCaddyConfigText(): Promise<string | null> {
   259→  try {
   260→    const response = await fetch(`${CADDY_ADMIN_URL}/config/`)
   261→    if (!response.ok) return null
   262→    return await response.text()
   263→  } catch {
   264→    return null
   265→  }
   266→}

---
name: memorytree-workflow
description: Detect, initialize, and maintain a reusable MemoryTree project-memory workspace for any code repository. On activation, immediately detect and report the repo's MemoryTree state.
---

# MemoryTree

Use this skill for repo-level project memory. Do not treat it as an application runtime feature unless the user explicitly asks to productize it.

## On Activation

When this skill is invoked, immediately perform these steps without waiting for further user input:

1. Detect the repo state (`not-installed`, `partial`, or `installed`) using `references/project-detection.md`.
2. Check `~/.memorytree/alerts.json`. If pending alerts exist, display them to the user before proceeding.
3. If `not-installed`: run `memorytree init` to scaffold the workspace, then report what was created.
4. If `partial`: run `memorytree upgrade` to add missing pieces, then report what was added.
5. If `installed`: read the active goal, bound todo, and latest chat log. Report the current state (goal summary, todo progress, pending tasks) and ask the user what they want to work on next. If `memorytree daemon status` shows the heartbeat is not registered, ask the user for their preferred heartbeat interval, auto_push preference, and scope, then offer to run `memorytree daemon install`. Use plain-text questions compatible with all AI assistants, not client-specific UI components.

Do not stop after detection to ask whether you should proceed. Act on the result immediately.

## Core Behavior

1. Detect the repo state before changing files. Use `references/project-detection.md`.
2. If MemoryTree is missing, initialize it with `memorytree init`. If the CLI is not available, create the files from `assets/templates/`.
3. If MemoryTree is partial, upgrade it with `memorytree upgrade` before manual maintenance.
4. If MemoryTree is already installed, maintain only the active goal, bound todo, and current chat log. Use `references/update-rules.md`.
5. Keep the installation compatible with the host repo's branch, PR, CI, and review rules. Use `references/git-policy.md`.
6. Prefer safe defaults: do not add reply suffix requirements unless the host repository already requires them, do not mix code-and-memory commits by default, and do not override branch policy. MemoryTree-only git automation is allowed only inside the isolated flow in `references/git-policy.md`.
7. When locale is not explicit, choose it from repo language first, then system language. Use `references/locale-selection.md`.
8. Keep reply language aligned with user language first, then repo locale. Use `references/response-language.md`.
9. For partial repos, use the non-destructive upgrade path before manual maintenance. Use `references/upgrade-path.md`.
10. When transcript archival is enabled, import transcripts with deterministic code, preserve raw transcripts as evidence in both the current repo mirror and the global archive, generate cleaned Markdown for indexing, keep cross-project backfills and ambiguous ownership cases in the global archive only, and ask once per repository whether raw transcript files may be committed or pushed. Use `references/transcript-archive.md`.
11. When CLI commands are needed, use `memorytree <subcommand>` (requires Node.js ≥ 20). If Node.js is not available, fall back to manual scaffolding from `assets/templates/`. See `references/execution-environment.md`.
12. Transcript discovery, import, cleaning, and push are handled by the background heartbeat process. The model only writes chat log summaries and updates goals and todos. See `references/heartbeat-scheduling.md`.
13. Global configuration is stored in `~/.memorytree/config.toml`. See `references/global-configuration.md`.
14. When the user asks to see their most recent conversation, trigger an on-demand transcript sync for the current project, locate the latest session across all three clients, and generate a continuation summary. See `references/transcript-archive.md` and `references/heartbeat-scheduling.md`.
15. All interactive prompts (heartbeat install, configuration, session continuity) must use plain-text questions compatible with every AI assistant that supports this skill. Do not rely on client-specific UI components. See `references/heartbeat-scheduling.md`.

## Read Order

1. Repo `AGENTS.md`, if present.
2. Latest file in `Memory/01_goals/`.
3. Latest todo bound to that goal in `Memory/02_todos/`.
4. `Memory/04_knowledge/` only when needed.
5. `Memory/06_transcripts/clean/`, transcript manifests, and repo-local raw transcript mirrors only when transcript history or cross-project memory search is relevant.
6. `Memory/03_chat_logs/` and `Memory/05_archive/` only when needed.

## Detect

1. Check whether `Memory/` exists and matches the layout in `references/memory-layout.md`.
2. Classify the repo as `not-installed`, `partial`, or `installed`.
3. If the repo already has stronger rules than the generated templates, preserve the repo rules and only add missing MemoryTree pieces.

## Upgrade

1. Use `memorytree upgrade` for repositories that already have `AGENTS.md`, custom policy files, or partial `Memory/` content.
2. Preserve existing repo policy files by default.
3. Create only the missing MemoryTree pieces.
4. Read the upgrade result and treat `agents_merge_required=true` as a manual review task, not an overwrite instruction.

## Initialize

1. Run `memorytree init --root <repo>` and pass `--project-name`, `--goal-summary`, and `--locale` when the user already provided them.
2. Use fresh init only when the repo does not already have `AGENTS.md` or another repo policy source such as a policy-bearing `CONTRIBUTING.md`, PR templates, `CODEOWNERS`, or commitlint config. If repo policy already exists, switch to `memorytree upgrade` instead of trying to skip `AGENTS.md`.
3. Review the generated `AGENTS.md` before keeping it. Merge it with the repo's existing policy if needed.
4. Keep the initial installation minimal: `Memory/01_goals`, `02_todos`, `03_chat_logs`, optional `04_knowledge`, `05_archive`, and `06_transcripts` only when transcript archival is enabled for the repo or needed for transcript import.
5. Use the locale-specific template files in `assets/templates/<locale>/` as the source of truth for first-run scaffolding.
6. Prefer `--locale auto` when the user did not request a language explicitly.
7. Use `memorytree locale` when you need a deterministic locale check without scaffolding files.
8. If Node.js is not available, create first-run files directly from `assets/templates/` instead of requiring a runtime installation.
9. If transcript archival is enabled for the repo, use `memorytree import --source <file>` for one explicit source file and `memorytree discover` when scanning local client stores. Matching transcripts must update both the repo mirror and the global archive, while unrelated projects, ambiguous ownership cases, or mismatched explicit sources are archived in the global archive only. Let the CLI generate cleaned transcripts deterministically without spending model tokens on the cleaning step.
10. Ask once whether raw transcript files may also be committed to the repository. Record the answer in `AGENTS.md`, keep the files in the repo either way, and exclude `raw` files from automatic staging until the user says yes.

## Maintain

1. Change the active goal only after explicit user confirmation of a scope or requirement change.
2. Update the active todo when progress changes, milestones move, or the next task becomes clearer.
3. Append chat logs only. Never rewrite or delete prior entries.
4. Keep active files small. Move stale context to archive or knowledge files instead of bloating the active goal or todo.

原因很简单：http://127.0.0.1:10010/projects/index.html 这个页面，不是“全局 heartbeat 已注册项目列表”，而是“当前这个报告站点里的项目页”。
现在 10010 上挂的是当前仓库这一个站点，Caddy 配置已经写死到 d-demo1-memorytree-workflow-d-demo1-memorytree-workflow.caddy (line 7) 和 d-demo1-memorytree-workflow-d-demo1-memorytree-workflow.caddy (line 10)，根目录就是 Memory/07_reports。
而这个 projects 页的生成逻辑，在 projects.ts (line 22) 里是从“当前报告加载到的 manifests”来算的；具体数据源是 build.ts (line 78) 和 build.ts (line 252)，只会读当前仓库下面的 Memory/06_transcripts/manifests。然后它再按 cwd 的最后一段分组，在 projects.ts (line 13) 和 projects.ts (line 35) 这里做，所以最后只显示出 memorytree-workflow 这 1 个项目。
所以：
• daemon status 里的 Projects: 3 = 机器级 heartbeat 当前注册了 3 个项目
• 10010/projects/index.html 里的 1 project(s) = 当前这个被 Caddy 暴露出来的单仓库报告里，只统计到了 1 个项目
这不是异常，按现在实现来说是正常现象。
如果你想，我下一步可以帮你做两种之一：
• 给 papaweb 也单独挂一个本地网页入口
• 设计一个“全局 3 项目总览页”，把注册的项目都汇总到一个页面里

逻辑不对把 这个地址不应该是全局项目的地址吗 请公允的判断一下
￼
￼
公允地说：你的直觉是有道理的，这里现在有“概念混淆”。
结论分两层：
1. 按当前代码实现来看，http://127.0.0.1:10010/projects/index.html 不是全局项目页，而是“当前这个仓库报告站点里的 projects 页”。
原因很明确：
• Caddy 现在把 10010 只指向了当前仓库的 Memory/07_reports；配置见 d-demo1-memorytree-workflow-d-demo1-memorytree-workflow.caddy (line 7) 和 d-demo1-memorytree-workflow-d-demo1-memorytree-workflow.caddy (line 10)
• 报告构建时只读取当前仓库下的 transcript manifests，见 build.ts (line 78) 和 build.ts (line 252)
• projects 页只是把这些 manifests 再按 cwd 末段分组，见 projects.ts (line 22) 和 projects.ts (line 35)
2. 但按产品理解和命名体验来看，你说“逻辑不对”也是成立的。
因为：
• heartbeat 是全局注册的，daemon status 里看到的是 3 个项目
• 页面名字却叫 Projects
• 用户很自然会理解成“全局项目列表”
• 实际上它显示的是“当前站点里出现过的项目分组”
所以我的公允判断是：
• 代码行为本身是自洽的，不是运行 bug
• 但产品语义和页面命名是有问题的，至少是明显误导
• 如果产品目标是“机器级 MemoryTree 总览”，那这个页面现在确实不对
• 如果产品目标只是“单仓库报告站点”，那实现没错，但 Projects 这个名字偏大，容易让人误会
我更倾向于把它定性为“产品/信息架构问题”，不是底层故障。
比较合理的改法有两种：
• 保守改法：把这个页改名成 Workspaces / Transcript Sources / Session Groups，明确它不是全局项目注册页
• 正向改法：新增一个真正的全局项目总览页，读取 ~/.memorytree/config.toml 或全局索引，把 3 个注册项目都列出来
如果你愿意，我下一步可以直接帮你做一次 review 结论文档，或者直接动手把这个逻辑改正确。

我们要正向改发，这个端口应该是全局项目 这样才能体系出这个skill 建立web服务价值 你看看这个 你理解一下我的需求

我理解你的需求了（虽然图片我看不到，但对话上下文已经足够清晰）。

你想要的是这个：

http://127.0.0.1:10010/                              ← 全局 Hub 总览页（所有注册项目）
http://127.0.0.1:10010/projects/memorytree-workflow/  ← memorytree-workflow 报告
http://127.0.0.1:10010/projects/papaweb/              ← papaweb 报告
http://127.0.0.1:10010/projects/openmnemo/            ← openmnemo 报告

现在是这个（错的）：

http://127.0.0.1:10010/                              ← 只有 memorytree-workflow 单项目站点
/projects/index.html                                  ← 只显示 1 个"项目"（实际是 transcript cwd 分组）

---

实现方案：

1. 新增 src/caddy/hub.ts — 读取 ~/.memorytree/config.toml，生成全局 Hub 静态 HTML 到 ~/.memorytree/hub/，每次 heartbeat 自动重建
2. 新增全局 Hub Caddy 片段 — 替换当前单项目片段，变成：
- / → ~/.memorytree/hub/index.html（全局总览）
- /projects/<name>/* → 各项目的 Memory/07_reports 目录（file_server）
3. 新增 CLI 命令 memorytree caddy enable-hub / disable-hub / hub-status

    46→export async function buildReport(options: BuildReportOptions): Promise<void> {
    47→  const { root, output } = options
    48→  const noAi = options.noAi ?? false
    49→  const model = options.model ?? DEFAULT_MODEL
    50→  const locale = options.locale ?? 'en'
    51→  const ghPagesBranch = options.ghPagesBranch ?? ''
    52→  const cname = options.cname ?? ''
    53→  const webhookUrl = options.webhookUrl ?? ''
    54→  const newSessionIds = options.newSessionIds ?? []
    55→  const reportBaseUrl = options.reportBaseUrl ?? ''
    56→
    57→  // Cache lives outside the gitignored output dir so it survives rm -rf
    58→  const cacheDir = join(root, 'Memory', '.report-cache')
    59→
    60→  // Load translations
    61→  const t: Translations = loadLocale(locale)
    62→
    63→  clearOutputDir(output)
    64→
    65→  // Ensure output dirs exist
    66→  mkdirSync(output, { recursive: true })
    67→  mkdirSync(join(output, 'transcripts'), { recursive: true })
    68→  mkdirSync(join(output, 'goals'), { recursive: true })
    69→  mkdirSync(join(output, 'knowledge'), { recursive: true })
    70→  mkdirSync(join(output, 'todos'), { recursive: true })
    71→  mkdirSync(join(output, 'archive'), { recursive: true })
    72→  mkdirSync(join(output, 'projects'), { recursive: true })
    73→  mkdirSync(cacheDir, { recursive: true })
    74→
    75→  // Ensure Memory/07_reports is gitignored
    76→  ensureGitignore(root, 'Memory/07_reports/')
    77→
    78→  // Load all manifests
    79→  const manifests = loadManifests(root)
    80→
    81→  // Build link graph from clean markdown
    82→  const linkGraph = buildLinkGraph(manifests, root)
    83→
    84→  // Accumulate tool counts while processing transcripts
    85→  let toolCounts: Record<string, number> = {}
    86→
    87→  // Summary options
    88→  const summaryOptions: SummaryOptions = { cacheDir, noAi, model }
    89→
    90→  // Process each transcript: parse → summarize → render → write → discard
    91→  const snippets: Record<string, string> = {}
    92→  const summaries: Record<string, string> = {}
    93→  const summaryPromises: Array<Promise<void>> = []
    94→
    95→  for (const m of manifests) {
    96→    const messages = parseCleanMarkdownMessages(m, root)
    97→
    98→    // Tool events from parsed transcript (try raw path)
    99→    const rawPath = resolveRawPath(m, root)
   100→    if (rawPath && existsSync(rawPath)) {
   101→      try {
   102→        const toolSummaries = extractToolSummariesFromRaw(rawPath, m.client)
   103→        const names = extractToolNames(toolSummaries)
   104→        toolCounts = accumulateToolCounts(toolCounts, names)
   105→      } catch {
   106→        // Skip if raw parsing fails
   107→      }
   108→    }
   109→
   110→    // Search snippet from first message text
   111→    const firstMsg = messages[0]
   112→    snippets[m.session_id] = firstMsg ? firstMsg.text.slice(0, 300) : ''
   113→
   114→    // Summarize + render (deferred to allow parallel API calls)
   115→    const manifest = m
   116→    const msgs = messages
   117→    summaryPromises.push(
   118→      (async () => {
   119→        try {
   120→        const summary = await getSummary(manifest.raw_sha256, msgs, summaryOptions)
   121→        summaries[manifest.session_id] = summary
   122→        const backlinkIds = linkGraph.backlinks[manifest.session_id] ?? []
   123→        const backlinkManifests = backlinkIds
   124→          .map(id => manifests.find(x => x.session_id === id))
   125→          .filter((x): x is ManifestEntry => x !== undefined)
   126→
   127→        const html = renderTranscript(msgs, manifest, summary, backlinkManifests, t, reportBaseUrl)
   128→        const outPath = transcriptOutputPath(output, manifest)
   129→        mkdirSync(dirname(outPath), { recursive: true })
   130→        writeFileSync(outPath, html, 'utf-8')
   131→        } catch (err: unknown) {
   132→          // eslint-disable-next-line no-console
   133→          getLogger().warn(`[build] Failed to render ${manifest.session_id}: ${String(err)}`)
   134→        }
   135→      })(),
   136→    )
   137→  }
   138→
   139→  // Wait for all transcript renders (parallel, bounded by semaphore in summarize.ts)
   140→  await Promise.all(summaryPromises)
   141→
   142→  // Extract tags in parallel (after summaries are ready)
   143→  const tagOptions = { cacheDir, noAi, model }
   144→  const tags: Record<string, string[]> = {}
   145→  await Promise.all(
   146→    manifests.map(async m => {
   147→      const summary = summaries[m.session_id] ?? ''
   148→      tags[m.session_id] = await getTags(m.raw_sha256, summary, tagOptions)
   149→    }),
   150→  )
   151→
   152→  // Compute final stats with accumulated tool counts
   153→  const stats = computeStats(manifests, toolCounts)
   154→
   155→  // Load markdown content for various pages
   156→  const goalFiles = loadMarkdownFiles(join(root, 'Memory', '01_goals'))
   157→  const todoFiles = loadMarkdownFiles(join(root, 'Memory', '02_todos'))
   158→  const knowledgeFiles = loadMarkdownFiles(join(root, 'Memory', '04_knowledge'))
   159→  const archiveFiles = loadMarkdownFiles(join(root, 'Memory', '05_archive'))
   160→
   161→  // Dashboard
   162→  writeFileSync(join(output, 'index.html'), renderDashboard(stats, manifests, t), 'utf-8')
   163→
   164→  // Session list
   165→  writeFileSync(
   166→    join(output, 'transcripts', 'index.html'),
   167→    renderTranscriptList(manifests, t, summaries, tags),
   168→    'utf-8',
   169→  )
   170→
   171→  // Goals page
   172→  writeFileSync(
   173→    join(output, 'goals', 'index.html'),
   174→    renderGoals(goalFiles, t),
   175→    'utf-8',
   176→  )
   177→
   178→  // Knowledge page
   179→  writeFileSync(
   180→    join(output, 'knowledge', 'index.html'),
   181→    renderKnowledge(knowledgeFiles, t),
   182→    'utf-8',
   183→  )
   184→
   185→  // Todos page
   186→  writeFileSync(
   187→    join(output, 'todos', 'index.html'),
   188→    renderTodos(todoFiles, t),
   189→    'utf-8',
   190→  )
   191→
   192→  // Archive page
   193→  writeFileSync(
   194→    join(output, 'archive', 'index.html'),
   195→    renderArchive(archiveFiles, t),
   196→    'utf-8',
   197→  )
   198→
   199→  // Projects page
   200→  writeFileSync(
   201→    join(output, 'projects', 'index.html'),
   202→    renderProjects(manifests, t),
   203→    'utf-8',
   204→  )
   205→
   206→  // Knowledge graph
   207→  writeFileSync(
   208→    join(output, 'graph.html'),
   209→    renderGraph(manifests, knowledgeFiles, linkGraph, t),
   210→    'utf-8',
   211→  )
   212→
   213→  // Search
   214→  const searchIndex = buildSearchIndex(manifests, m => snippets[m.session_id] ?? '')
   215→  writeFileSync(join(output, 'search.html'), renderSearchPage(searchIndex, t), 'utf-8')
   216→
   217→  // RSS Feed
   218→  writeFileSync(join(output, 'feed.xml'), renderRssFeed(manifests, summaries, reportBaseUrl), 'utf-8')
   219→
   220→  // GitHub Pages deployment (non-blocking on failure)
   221→  if (ghPagesBranch) {
   222→    try {
   223→      const { deployGithubPages } = await import('./deploy/github-pages.js')
   224→      await deployGithubPages({ repoRoot: root, outputDir: output, branch: ghPagesBranch, cname })
   225→    } catch {
   226→      // Logged inside deployGithubPages
   227→    }
   228→  } else if (cname) {
   229→    // Write CNAME even without deploy (writeFileSync already imported at top)
   230→    writeFileSync(join(output, 'CNAME'), cname + '\n', 'utf-8')
   231→  }
   232→
   233→  // Webhook notification (non-blocking on failure)
   234→  if (webhookUrl) {
   235→    try {
   236→      const { sendWebhook } = await import('./deploy/webhook.js')
   237→      await sendWebhook({
   238→        url: webhookUrl,
   239→        sessionCount: manifests.length,
   240→        newSessionIds,
   241→      })
   242→    } catch {
   243→      // Logged inside sendWebhook
   244→    }
   245→  }
   246→}

   248→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   249→// Manifest loading
   250→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   251→
   252→function loadManifests(root: string): ManifestEntry[] {
   253→  const manifestsDir = join(root, 'Memory', '06_transcripts', 'manifests')
   254→  if (!existsSync(manifestsDir)) return []
   255→
   256→  const manifests: ManifestEntry[] = []
   257→  loadManifestsRecursive(manifestsDir, manifests)
   258→  return manifests
   259→}
   260→
   261→function loadManifestsRecursive(dir: string, out: ManifestEntry[]): void {
   262→  let entries: string[]
   263→  try {
   264→    entries = readdirSync(dir)
   265→  } catch {
   266→    return
   267→  }
   268→
   269→  for (const entry of entries) {
   270→    const fullPath = join(dir, entry)
   271→    if (entry.endsWith('.json')) {
   272→      try {
   273→        const raw = readFileSync(fullPath, 'utf-8')
   274→        const parsed: unknown = JSON.parse(raw)
   275→        if (
   276→          parsed !== null &&
   277→          typeof parsed === 'object' &&
   278→          typeof (parsed as Record<string, unknown>)['session_id'] === 'string' &&
   279→          typeof (parsed as Record<string, unknown>)['client'] === 'string'
   280→        ) {
   281→          out.push(parsed as ManifestEntry)
   282→        }
   283→      } catch {
   284→        // Skip malformed manifests
   285→      }
   286→    } else {
   287→      // Recurse into subdirectories
   288→      loadManifestsRecursive(fullPath, out)
   289→    }
   290→  }
   291→}
   292→
   293→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   294→// Clean markdown message parsing
   295→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   296→
   297→/** Parse messages from a clean markdown file. */
   298→export function parseCleanMarkdownMessages(m: ManifestEntry, root: string): RenderedMessage[] {
   299→  const cleanPath = m.repo_clean_path
   300→    ? join(root, m.repo_clean_path)
   301→    : m.global_clean_path
   302→  if (!cleanPath || !existsSync(cleanPath)) return []
   303→
   304→  let content: string
   305→  try {
   306→    content = readFileSync(cleanPath, 'utf-8')
   307→  } catch {
   308→    return []
   309→  }
   310→
   311→  return parseMessagesFromMarkdown(content)
   312→}
   313→
   314→/** Extract role/timestamp/text from clean markdown format. */
   315→export function parseMessagesFromMarkdown(content: string): RenderedMessage[] {
   316→  const messages: RenderedMessage[] = []
   317→
   318→  // Find ## Messages section
   319→  const msgSection = content.indexOf('\n## Messages')
   320→  if (msgSection === -1) return []
   321→
   322→  const body = content.slice(msgSection + 12) // after "## Messages\n"
   323→
   324→  // Split on ### N. role headers
   325→  const msgRe = /^### \d+\.\s+(\w+)/gm
   326→  let match: RegExpExecArray | null
   327→  const starts: Array<{ index: number; role: string }> = []
   328→
   329→  while ((match = msgRe.exec(body)) !== null) {
   330→    starts.push({ index: match.index, role: match[1] ?? 'unknown' })
   331→  }
   332→
   333→  for (let i = 0; i < starts.length; i++) {
   334→    const start = starts[i]
   335→    if (!start) continue
   336→    const nextStart = starts[i + 1]
   337→    const chunk = nextStart
   338→      ? body.slice(start.index, nextStart.index)
   339→      : body.slice(start.index)
   340→
   341→    const lines = chunk.split('\n')
   342→    // First line is the header, second may be timestamp
   343→    let timestamp = ''
   344→    const textLines: string[] = []
   345→    let pastHeader = false
   346→
   347→    for (const line of lines) {
   348→      if (!pastHeader && line.startsWith('### ')) {
   349→        pastHeader = true
   350→        continue
   351→      }
   352→      if (!pastHeader) continue
   353→      const tsMatch = line.match(/^- Timestamp:\s*`([^`]+)`/)
   354→      if (tsMatch && !timestamp) {
   355→        timestamp = tsMatch[1] ?? ''
   356→        continue
   357→      }
   358→      textLines.push(line)
   359→    }
   360→
   361→    // Remove leading/trailing blank lines from text
   362→    const text = textLines.join('\n').trim()
   363→    if (text || timestamp) {
   364→      messages.push({ role: start.role, timestamp, text })
   365→    }
   366→  }
   367→
   368→  return messages
   369→}
   370→
   371→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   372→// Raw transcript tool extraction
   373→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   374→
   375→/** Best-effort extraction of tool event summaries from a raw JSONL file. */
   376→function extractToolSummariesFromRaw(rawPath: string, _client: string): string[] {
   377→  const summaries: string[] = []
   378→  let content: string
   379→  try {
   380→    content = readFileSync(rawPath, 'utf-8')
   381→  } catch {
   382→    return []
   383→  }
   384→
   385→  for (const line of content.split('\n')) {
   386→    const trimmed = line.trim()
   387→    if (!trimmed) continue
   388→    try {
   389→      const record = JSON.parse(trimmed) as Record<string, unknown>
   390→      // Codex: function_call type
   391→      const type = record['type'] as string | undefined
   392→      if (type === 'function_call' || type === 'custom_tool_call') {
   393→        const name = (record['name'] as string | undefined) ?? type
   394→        summaries.push(name)
   395→        continue
   396→      }
   397→      // Claude: tool_use content blocks
   398→      const payload = record['message'] as Record<string, unknown> | undefined
   399→      const content2 = (payload?.['content'] ?? record['content']) as unknown[] | undefined
   400→      if (Array.isArray(content2)) {
   401→        for (const block of content2) {
   402→          if (
   403→            block !== null &&
   404→            typeof block === 'object' &&
   405→            (block as Record<string, unknown>)['type'] === 'tool_use'
   406→          ) {
   407→            const name = ((block as Record<string, unknown>)['name'] as string | undefined) ?? 'tool_use'
   408→            summaries.push(name)
   409→          }
   410→        }
   411→      }
   412→    } catch {
   413→      // Skip malformed lines
   414→    }
   415→  }
   416→
   417→  return summaries
   418→}
   419→
   420→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   421→// Output path helpers
   422→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   423→
   424→function transcriptOutputPath(output: string, m: ManifestEntry): string {
   425→  const cleanPath = m.repo_clean_path || m.global_clean_path || ''
   426→  const stem = cleanPath ? basename(cleanPath, '.md') : m.session_id
   427→  return join(output, 'transcripts', m.client, `${stem}.html`)
   428→}
   429→
   430→function resolveRawPath(m: ManifestEntry, root: string): string | null {
   431→  if (m.repo_raw_path) {
   432→    return join(root, m.repo_raw_path)
   433→  }
   434→  if (m.global_raw_path) {
   435→    return m.global_raw_path
   436→  }
   437→  return null
   438→}
   439→
   440→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   441→// Markdown file loader (for goals/knowledge/todos/archive)
   442→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   443→
   444→function loadMarkdownFiles(dir: string): Array<{ filename: string; title: string; content: string }> {
   445→  if (!existsSync(dir)) return []
   446→
   447→  let entries: string[]
   448→  try {
   449→    entries = readdirSync(dir)
   450→  } catch {
   451→    return []
   452→  }
   453→
   454→  return entries
   455→    .filter(e => e.endsWith('.md'))
   456→    .sort()
   457→    .map(filename => {
   458→      const fullPath = join(dir, filename)
   459→      let content = ''
   460→      try {
   461→        content = readFileSync(fullPath, 'utf-8')
   462→      } catch {
   463→        // empty
   464→      }
   465→      const title = extractMarkdownTitle(content) || basename(filename, '.md')
   466→      return { filename, title, content }
   467→    })
   468→}
   469→
   470→function clearOutputDir(output: string): void {
   471→  if (!existsSync(output)) return
   472→
   473→  let entries: string[]
   474→  try {
   475→    entries = readdirSync(output)
   476→  } catch {
   477→    return
   478→  }
   479→
   480→  for (const entry of entries) {
   481→    try {
   482→      rmSync(join(output, entry), { recursive: true, force: true })
   483→    } catch {
   484→      // Best-effort cleanup
   485→    }
   486→  }
   487→}
   488→
   489→function extractMarkdownTitle(content: string): string {
   490→  const match = content.match(/^#\s+(.+)$/m)
   491→  return match?.[1]?.trim() ?? ''
   492→}
   493→
   494→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   495→// .gitignore management
   496→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   497→
   498→export function ensureGitignore(root: string, entry: string): void {
   499→  const gitignorePath = join(root, '.gitignore')
   500→  let existing = ''
   501→  if (existsSync(gitignorePath)) {
   502→    try {
   503→      existing = readFileSync(gitignorePath, 'utf-8')
   504→    } catch {
   505→      return
   506→    }
   507→  }
   508→  // Check if already present (normalize line endings)
   509→  const lines = existing.replace(/\r\n/g, '\n').split('\n')
   510→  if (lines.some(l => l.trim() === entry.trim())) return
   511→
   512→  // Append with trailing newline
   513→  const append = existing.endsWith('\n') ? entry + '\n' : '\n' + entry + '\n'
   514→  try {
   515→    appendFileSync(gitignorePath, append, 'utf-8')
   516→  } catch {
   517→    // Best-effort
   518→  }
   519→}

    45→  /(?:api[_-]?key|apikey)\s*[:=]\s*\S+/i,
    46→  /(?:password|passwd|pwd)\s*[:=]\s*\S+/i,

    54→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    55→// Main entry point

    58→export interface HeartbeatRunOptions {
    59→  readonly force?: boolean
    60→  readonly root?: string
    61→}
    62→
    63→export async function main(options: HeartbeatRunOptions = {}): Promise<number> {
    64→  const config = loadConfig()
    65→  setupLogging(config.log_level as LogLevel)
    66→  const logger = getLogger()
    67→
    68→  if (!acquireLock()) {
    69→    logger.info('Another heartbeat instance is running. Exiting.')
    70→    writeAlert('global', 'lock_held', 'Heartbeat exited: another instance held the lock.')
    71→    return 0
    72→  }
    73→
    74→  try {
    75→    return await runHeartbeat(config, options)
    76→  } finally {
    77→    releaseLock()
    78→  }
    79→}
    80→
    81→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    82→// Heartbeat orchestration
    83→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    84→
    85→export async function runHeartbeat(config: Config, options: HeartbeatRunOptions = {}): Promise<number> {
    86→  const logger = getLogger()
    87→  const targetProject = options.root ? findProjectForPath(config, resolve(options.root)) : null
    88→
    89→  if (config.projects.length === 0) {
    90→    logger.info('No projects registered in config.toml. Nothing to do.')
    91→    return 0
    92→  }
    93→  if (options.root && !targetProject) {
    94→    logger.warn(`No registered project matched: ${resolve(options.root)}`)
    95→    return 1
    96→  }
    97→
    98→  const projects = targetProject ? [targetProject] : config.projects
    99→
   100→  logger.info(`Heartbeat started. ${projects.length} project(s) selected.`)
   101→
   102→  let nextConfig = config
   103→  let configChanged = false
   104→  const now = new Date()
   105→  const runTimestamp = now.toISOString()
   106→
   107→  for (const entry of projects) {
   108→    const projectName = projectDisplayName(entry)
   109→    const projectPath = resolve(projectExecutionPath(entry))
   110→    const heartbeatDue = options.force === true || projectIsDue(entry, now)
   111→    const refreshDue = options.force === true || projectRefreshIsDue(entry, now)
   112→
   113→    if (!heartbeatDue && !refreshDue) {
   114→      logger.debug(`[${projectName}] Not due yet, skipping.`)
   115→      continue
   116→    }
   117→
   118→    try {
   119→      const worktree = ensureProjectWorktree(entry)
   120→      if (!existsSync(projectPath)) {
   121→        logger.warn(`Project path does not exist, skipping: ${projectPath}`)
   122→        continue
   123→      }
   124→
   125→      if (worktree.created) {
   126→        logger.info(`[${projectName}] Created worktree on branch '${worktree.branch}'.`)
   127→      }
   128→
   129→      if (heartbeatDue) {
   130→        const contextSync = syncProjectContextToMemory(entry)
   131→        if (!contextSync.skipped) {
   132→          logger.info(
   133→            `[${projectName}] Synced context to ${worktree.branch} ` +
   134→            `(copied ${contextSync.copied}, deleted ${contextSync.deleted}).`,
   135→          )
   136→        }
   137→
   138→        await processProject(config, projectPath, projectName, entry)
   139→        nextConfig = noteProjectHeartbeatRun(nextConfig, entry.id, runTimestamp)
   140→        configChanged = true
   141→      }
   142→
   143→      if (heartbeatDue || refreshDue) {
   144→        const outputSync = syncProjectOutputsToDevelopment(entry)
   145→        if (!outputSync.skipped) {
   146→          logger.info(
   147→            `[${projectName}] Synced outputs back to development directory ` +
   148→            `(copied ${outputSync.copied}, deleted ${outputSync.deleted}).`,
   149→          )
   150→        }
   151→        nextConfig = noteProjectRefreshRun(nextConfig, entry.id, runTimestamp)
   152→        configChanged = true
   153→      }
   154→    } catch (err: unknown) {
   155→      logger.exception(`Error processing project: ${projectPath}`, err)
   156→      writeAlertWithThreshold(
   157→        toPosixPath(projectPath),
   158→        'push_failed',
   159→        `Heartbeat error for project: ${basename(projectPath)}`,
   160→      )
   161→    }
   162→  }
   163→
   164→  if (configChanged) {
   165→    saveConfig(nextConfig)
   166→  }
   167→
   168→  logger.info('Heartbeat finished.')
   169→  return 0
   170→}

   172→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   173→// Per-project processing
   174→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   175→
   176→export async function processProject(
   177→  config: Config,
   178→  projectPath: string,
   179→  projectName: string,
   180→  project?: ProjectEntry,
   181→): Promise<void> {
   182→  const logger = getLogger()
   183→  const repoSlug = slugify(projectName, 'project')
   184→  const globalRoot = defaultGlobalTranscriptRoot()
   185→  const branch = currentBranch(projectPath)
   186→  const mirrorToRepo = isDedicatedMemorytreeBranch(branch, project)
   187→  const autoPush = project?.auto_push ?? config.auto_push ?? true
   188→  const generateReport = project?.generate_report ?? config.generate_report ?? false
   189→  const aiSummaryModel = project?.ai_summary_model ?? config.ai_summary_model ?? 'claude-haiku-4-5-20251001'
   190→  const locale = project?.locale ?? config.locale ?? 'en'
   191→  const ghPagesBranch = project?.gh_pages_branch ?? config.gh_pages_branch ?? ''
   192→  const cname = project?.cname ?? config.cname ?? ''
   193→  const webhookUrl = project?.webhook_url ?? config.webhook_url ?? ''
   194→  const reportBaseUrl = project?.report_base_url ?? config.report_base_url ?? ''
   195→
   196→  if (!mirrorToRepo) {
   197→    logger.warn(
   198→      `[${projectName}] Current branch '${branch}' is not a dedicated MemoryTree branch. ` +
   199→      'Importing to the global archive only.',
   200→    )
   201→  }
   202→
   203→  const discovered = discoverSourceFiles()
   204→  let importedCount = 0
   205→
   206→  for (const [client, source] of discovered) {
   207→    let parsed: ParsedTranscript
   208→    try {
   209→      parsed = parseTranscript(client, source)
   210→    } catch {
   211→      logger.debug(`Failed to parse ${source}, skipping.`)
   212→      continue
   213→    }
   214→
   215→    if (!transcriptHasContent(parsed)) continue
   216→    if (!transcriptMatchesRepo(parsed, projectPath, repoSlug)) continue
   217→
   218→    scanSensitive(parsed, projectPath)
   219→
   220→    try {
   221→      await importTranscript(parsed, projectPath, globalRoot, repoSlug, 'not-set', mirrorToRepo)
   222→      importedCount++
   223→    } catch {
   224→      logger.exception(`Failed to import transcript: ${source}`)
   225→    }
   226→  }
   227→
   228→  if (importedCount === 0) {
   229→    logger.info(`[${projectName}] No new transcripts to import.`)
   230→    return
   231→  }
   232→
   233→  logger.info(`[${projectName}] Imported ${importedCount} transcript(s).`)
   234→  if (mirrorToRepo) {
   235→    gitCommitAndPush({ auto_push: autoPush }, projectPath, projectName, importedCount)
   236→  } else {
   237→    logger.info(`[${projectName}] Skipped repo-local commit/push on branch '${branch}'.`)
   238→  }
   239→
   240→  if (generateReport) {
   241→    try {
   242→      const { buildReport } = await import('../report/build.js')
   243→      await buildReport({
   244→        root: projectPath,
   245→        output: join(projectPath, 'Memory', '07_reports'),
   246→        noAi: !process.env['ANTHROPIC_API_KEY'],
   247→        model: aiSummaryModel,
   248→        locale,
   249→        ghPagesBranch,
   250→        cname,
   251→        webhookUrl,
   252→        reportBaseUrl,
   253→      })
   254→      logger.info(`[${projectName}] Report generated.`)
   255→    } catch (err: unknown) {
   256→      logger.warn(`[${projectName}] Report generation failed: ${String(err)}`)
   257→      // Never propagate — report failure must not abort heartbeat cycle
   258→    }
   259→  }
   260→}
   261→
   262→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   263→// Sensitive pattern scanning
   264→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   265→
   266→export function scanSensitive(parsed: ParsedTranscript, projectPath: string): void {
   267→  const logger = getLogger()
   268→  for (const msg of parsed.messages) {
   269→    for (const pattern of SENSITIVE_PATTERNS) {
   270→      if (pattern.test(msg.text)) {
   271→        logger.warn(
   272→          `Sensitive pattern detected in transcript ${parsed.source_path} (project: ${basename(projectPath)}, role: ${msg.role})`,
   273→        )
   274→        writeAlert(
   275→          toPosixPath(projectPath),
   276→          'sensitive_match',
   277→          `Sensitive pattern in transcript: ${basename(parsed.source_path)}`,
   278→        )
   279→        return
   280→      }
   281→    }
   282→  }
   283→}
   284→
   285→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   286→// Git operations
   287→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   288→
   289→export function gitCommitAndPush(
   290→  config: Pick<Config, 'auto_push'>,
   291→  projectPath: string,
   292→  projectName: string,
   293→  count: number,
   294→): void {
   295→  const logger = getLogger()
   296→
   297→  const changedPaths = changedMemoryPaths(projectPath)
   298→  if (changedPaths.length === 0) {
   299→    logger.info(`[${projectName}] No git changes in Memory/.`)
   300→    return
   301→  }
   302→
   303→  const stageablePaths = changedPaths.filter(path => !isRepoRawTranscriptPath(path))
   304→  if (stageablePaths.length === 0) {
   305→    logger.info(`[${projectName}] Only raw transcript mirror changes detected; skipping commit.`)
   306→    return
   307→  }
   308→
   309→  git(projectPath, 'add', '--', ...stageablePaths)
   310→  git(projectPath, 'commit', '-m', `memorytree(transcripts): import ${count} transcript(s)`)
   311→  logger.info(`[${projectName}] Committed ${count} transcript import(s).`)
   312→
   313→  if (!config.auto_push) {
   314→    logger.info(`[${projectName}] auto_push disabled, skipping push.`)
   315→    return
   316→  }
   317→
   318→  const remotes = git(projectPath, 'remote')
   319→  if (!remotes.trim()) {
   320→    logger.warn(`[${projectName}] No git remote configured, skipping push.`)
   321→    writeAlert(toPosixPath(projectPath), 'no_remote', 'Push skipped: no Git remote configured.')
   322→    return
   323→  }
   324→
   325→  if (!tryPush(projectPath, projectName)) {
   326→    logger.warn(`[${projectName}] Push failed, retrying once...`)
   327→    if (!tryPush(projectPath, projectName)) {
   328→      logger.error(`[${projectName}] Push failed after retry.`)
   329→      writeAlertWithThreshold(toPosixPath(projectPath), 'push_failed', 'Push failed after retry.')
   330→      return
   331→    }
   332→  }
   333→
   334→  resetFailureCount(toPosixPath(projectPath), 'push_failed')
   335→}
   336→
   337→export function tryPush(projectPath: string, projectName: string): boolean {
   338→  try {
   339→    const branch = currentBranch(projectPath)
   340→    if (hasTrackingUpstream(projectPath)) {
   341→      git(projectPath, 'push')
   342→    } else {
   343→      const upstream = ensureBranchUpstream(projectPath, branch)
   344→      if (upstream.remote === null) {
   345→        return false
   346→      }
   347→      getLogger().info(`[${projectName}] Configured upstream ${upstream.remote}/${branch}.`)
   348→    }
   349→    getLogger().info(`[${projectName}] Pushed successfully.`)
   350→    return true
   351→  } catch {
   352→    return false
   353→  }
   354→}
   355→
   356→export function currentBranch(projectPath: string): string {
   357→  return git(projectPath, 'rev-parse', '--abbrev-ref', 'HEAD').trim()
   358→}
   359→
   360→export function isDedicatedMemorytreeBranch(
   361→  branch: string,
   362→  project?: Pick<ProjectEntry, 'memory_branch'>,
   363→): boolean {
   364→  return isProjectMemoryBranch(branch, project)
   365→}
   366→
   367→export function changedMemoryPaths(projectPath: string): string[] {
   368→  const status = git(projectPath, 'status', '--porcelain', '--untracked-files=all', '--', 'Memory/')
   369→  const seen = new Set<string>()
   370→  const paths: string[] = []
   371→
   372→  for (const rawLine of status.split(/\r?\n/)) {
   373→    const path = statusLinePath(rawLine)
   374→    if (path === null || seen.has(path)) continue
   375→    seen.add(path)
   376→    paths.push(path)
   377→  }
   378→
   379→  return paths
   380→}
   381→
   382→export function isRepoRawTranscriptPath(path: string): boolean {
   383→  return path.replace(/\\/g, '/').startsWith(RAW_TRANSCRIPT_PREFIX)
   384→}
   385→
   386→function statusLinePath(line: string): string | null {
   387→  if (line.length < 4) return null
   388→
   389→  const rawPath = line.slice(3).trim()
   390→  if (!rawPath) return null
   391→
   392→  const path = rawPath.includes(' -> ')
   393→    ? rawPath.slice(rawPath.lastIndexOf(' -> ') + 4)
   394→    : rawPath
   395→
   396→  return unquotePath(path)
   397→}
   398→
   399→function unquotePath(path: string): string {
   400→  if (!(path.startsWith('"') && path.endsWith('"'))) return path
   401→
   402→  return path
   403→    .slice(1, -1)
   404→    .replace(/\\"/g, '"')
   405→    .replace(/\\\\/g, '\\')
   406→}
   407→

    46→export async function buildReport(options: BuildReportOptions): Promise<void> {

    50→  const locale = options.locale ?? 'en'
    51→  const ghPagesBranch = options.ghPagesBranch ?? ''

    63→  clearOutputDir(output)

    68→  mkdirSync(join(output, 'goals'), { recursive: true })
    69→  mkdirSync(join(output, 'knowledge'), { recursive: true })
    70→  mkdirSync(join(output, 'todos'), { recursive: true })
    71→  mkdirSync(join(output, 'archive'), { recursive: true })
    72→  mkdirSync(join(output, 'projects'), { recursive: true })

    86→
    87→  // Summary options
    88→  const summaryOptions: SummaryOptions = { cacheDir, noAi, model }
    89→

    91→  const snippets: Record<string, string> = {}
    92→  const summaries: Record<string, string> = {}
    93→  const summaryPromises: Array<Promise<void>> = []
    94→
    95→  for (const m of manifests) {
    96→    const messages = parseCleanMarkdownMessages(m, root)
    97→
    98→    // Tool events from parsed transcript (try raw path)
    99→    const rawPath = resolveRawPath(m, root)
   100→    if (rawPath && existsSync(rawPath)) {
   101→      try {
   102→        const toolSummaries = extractToolSummariesFromRaw(rawPath, m.client)
   103→        const names = extractToolNames(toolSummaries)
   104→        toolCounts = accumulateToolCounts(toolCounts, names)
   105→      } catch {
   106→        // Skip if raw parsing fails
   107→      }
   108→    }

   111→    const firstMsg = messages[0]
   112→    snippets[m.session_id] = firstMsg ? firstMsg.text.slice(0, 300) : ''
   113→

   115→    const manifest = m
   116→    const msgs = messages
   117→    summaryPromises.push(
   118→      (async () => {
   119→        try {
   120→        const summary = await getSummary(manifest.raw_sha256, msgs, summaryOptions)
   121→        summaries[manifest.session_id] = summary
   122→        const backlinkIds = linkGraph.backlinks[manifest.session_id] ?? []
   123→        const backlinkManifests = backlinkIds

   126→

   128→        const outPath = transcriptOutputPath(output, manifest)
   129→        mkdirSync(dirname(outPath), { recursive: true })
   130→        writeFileSync(outPath, html, 'utf-8')
   131→        } catch (err: unknown) {
   132→          // eslint-disable-next-line no-console
   133→          getLogger().warn(`[build] Failed to render ${manifest.session_id}: ${String(err)}`)
   134→        }
   135→      })(),
   136→    )
   137→  }
   138→
   139→  // Wait for all transcript renders (parallel, bounded by semaphore in summarize.ts)
   140→  await Promise.all(summaryPromises)
   141→
   142→  // Extract tags in parallel (after summaries are ready)
   143→  const tagOptions = { cacheDir, noAi, model }
   144→  const tags: Record<string, string[]> = {}

   146→    manifests.map(async m => {
   147→      const summary = summaries[m.session_id] ?? ''
   148→      tags[m.session_id] = await getTags(m.raw_sha256, summary, tagOptions)

    13→export interface CmdReportBuildOptions {

    43→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    44→// Serve command
    45→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    46→
    47→export interface CmdReportServeOptions {
    48→  dir: string
    49→  port: number
    50→}
    51→
    52→export function cmdReportServe(opts: CmdReportServeOptions): number {
    53→  const root = resolve(opts.dir)
    54→  const port = opts.port
    55→
    56→  const MIME: Record<string, string> = {
    57→    '.html': 'text/html; charset=utf-8',
    58→    '.css': 'text/css',
    59→    '.js': 'application/javascript',
    60→    '.json': 'application/json',
    61→    '.svg': 'image/svg+xml',
    62→    '.ico': 'image/x-icon',
    63→  }
    64→
    65→  const server = createServer((req, res) => {
    66→    let urlPath: string
    67→    try {
    68→      urlPath = decodeURIComponent((req.url ?? '/').split('?')[0] ?? '/')
    69→    } catch {
    70→      res.writeHead(400, { 'Content-Type': 'text/plain' })
    71→      res.end('Bad request')
    72→      return
    73→    }
    74→
    75→    let filePath = join(root, urlPath)
    76→
    77→    // Containment check: reject paths that escape the serve root
    78→    // Use sep (\ on Windows, / on Unix) so the check works cross-platform.
    79→    if (!filePath.startsWith(root + sep) && filePath !== root) {
    80→      res.writeHead(403, { 'Content-Type': 'text/plain' })
    81→      res.end('Forbidden')
    82→      return
    83→    }
    84→
    85→    // Serve index.html for directory requests
    86→    if (existsSync(filePath) && statSync(filePath).isDirectory()) {
    87→      filePath = join(filePath, 'index.html')
    88→    }
    89→
    90→    if (!existsSync(filePath)) {
    91→      res.writeHead(404, { 'Content-Type': 'text/plain' })
    92→      res.end('Not found')
    93→      return
    94→    }
    95→
    96→    const ext = extname(filePath)
    97→    const contentType = MIME[ext] ?? 'application/octet-stream'
    98→    res.writeHead(200, { 'Content-Type': contentType })
    99→    const stream = createReadStream(filePath)
   100→    stream.on('error', () => { res.destroy() })
   101→    stream.pipe(res)
   102→  })
   103→
   104→  server.on('error', (err: NodeJS.ErrnoException) => {
   105→    if (err.code === 'EADDRINUSE') {
   106→      console.error(`Error: port ${port} is already in use.`)
   107→      process.exit(1)
   108→    }
   109→    console.error(`Server error: ${String(err)}`)
   110→    process.exit(1)
   111→  })
   112→
   113→  server.listen(port, () => {
   114→    console.log('Temporary local preview server started.')
   115→    console.log('For long-running local access, prefer Caddy hosting this directory.')
   116→    console.log(`Serving ${root}`)
   117→    console.log(`Open: http://localhost:${port}/`)
   118→    console.log('Press Ctrl+C to stop.')
   119→  })
   120→
   121→  return 0
   122→}

    63→export async function main(options: HeartbeatRunOptions = {}): Promise<number> {
    64→  const config = loadConfig()

    66→  const logger = getLogger()
    67→
    68→  if (!acquireLock()) {
    69→    logger.info('Another heartbeat instance is running. Exiting.')

    77→    releaseLock()

    81→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

    85→export async function runHeartbeat(config: Config, options: HeartbeatRunOptions = {}): Promise<number> {
    86→  const logger = getLogger()
    87→  const targetProject = options.root ? findProjectForPath(config, resolve(options.root)) : null
    88→
    89→  if (config.projects.length === 0) {
    90→    logger.info('No projects registered in config.toml. Nothing to do.')
    91→    return 0
    92→  }
    93→  if (options.root && !targetProject) {
    94→    logger.warn(`No registered project matched: ${resolve(options.root)}`)
    95→    return 1
    96→  }
    97→
    98→  const projects = targetProject ? [targetProject] : config.projects
    99→
   100→  logger.info(`Heartbeat started. ${projects.length} project(s) selected.`)
   101→
   102→  let nextConfig = config
   103→  let configChanged = false
   104→  const now = new Date()
   105→  const runTimestamp = now.toISOString()
   106→
   107→  for (const entry of projects) {
   108→    const projectName = projectDisplayName(entry)
   109→    const projectPath = resolve(projectExecutionPath(entry))
   110→    const heartbeatDue = options.force === true || projectIsDue(entry, now)
   111→    const refreshDue = options.force === true || projectRefreshIsDue(entry, now)
   112→
   113→    if (!heartbeatDue && !refreshDue) {
   114→      logger.debug(`[${projectName}] Not due yet, skipping.`)
   115→      continue
   116→    }
   117→
   118→    try {
   119→      const worktree = ensureProjectWorktree(entry)
   120→      if (!existsSync(projectPath)) {
   121→        logger.warn(`Project path does not exist, skipping: ${projectPath}`)
   122→        continue
   123→      }
   124→
   125→      if (worktree.created) {
   126→        logger.info(`[${projectName}] Created worktree on branch '${worktree.branch}'.`)
   127→      }
   128→
   129→      if (heartbeatDue) {
   130→        const contextSync = syncProjectContextToMemory(entry)
   131→        if (!contextSync.skipped) {
   132→          logger.info(
   133→            `[${projectName}] Synced context to ${worktree.branch} ` +
   134→            `(copied ${contextSync.copied}, deleted ${contextSync.deleted}).`,
   135→          )
   136→        }
   137→
   138→        await processProject(config, projectPath, projectName, entry)
   139→        nextConfig = noteProjectHeartbeatRun(nextConfig, entry.id, runTimestamp)
   140→        configChanged = true
   141→      }
   142→
   143→      if (heartbeatDue || refreshDue) {
   144→        const outputSync = syncProjectOutputsToDevelopment(entry)
   145→        if (!outputSync.skipped) {
   146→          logger.info(
   147→            `[${projectName}] Synced outputs back to development directory ` +
   148→            `(copied ${outputSync.copied}, deleted ${outputSync.deleted}).`,
   149→          )
   150→        }
   151→        nextConfig = noteProjectRefreshRun(nextConfig, entry.id, runTimestamp)
   152→        configChanged = true
   153→      }
   154→    } catch (err: unknown) {
   155→      logger.exception(`Error processing project: ${projectPath}`, err)
   156→      writeAlertWithThreshold(
   157→        toPosixPath(projectPath),
   158→        'push_failed',
   159→        `Heartbeat error for project: ${basename(projectPath)}`,
   160→      )
   161→    }
   162→  }
   163→
   164→  if (configChanged) {
   165→    saveConfig(nextConfig)
   166→  }
   167→
   168→  logger.info('Heartbeat finished.')
   169→  return 0
   170→}

assistant #93 10:02:41

现在我对整个项目有了足够清晰的认识，来做一个公允的方案评估。

---

## 重新审视你的需求

你的需求本质是：10010 端口应该是机器级 MemoryTree 控制台，能看到所有注册项目，而不是某一个项目的单独报告站点。

---

## 我上一个方案的问题

我之前提的方案（新建 src/caddy/hub.ts + 全局 Hub 页 + 新 CLI 命令）方向对，但架构选择有问题：

- 新建一套独立的静态 HTML 生成器，CSS/样式体系和现有报告完全割裂
- 用 Caddy path prefix 路由各项目 (/projects/<name>/*) 是可行的，但把"全局总览"和"单项目报告"混在同一个 Caddy 站点里，会让报告内的相对路径链接全部失效（报告里的 ../transcripts/xxx 会变成错误路径）
- 增加新的 CLI 子命令是过度工程，用户不需要手动管理 hub

---

## 更好的方案

项目里已经有一套完整的报告渲染体系（CSS、layout、i18n、dashboard、projects 页），而且 buildReport 本身就支持 root + output 分离。

正确做法：让现有报告系统本身支持"全局模式"

### 核心改动

1. buildReport 新增全局模式 — 读取 ~/.memorytree/config.toml 里的所有项目，把各项目的 manifests 合并进来，cwd 信息天然就能在 projects.ts 里分组出多个项目

2. Caddy 片段不变 — 10010 仍然只指向一个目录，但那个目录是"全局报告"的输出目录（比如 ~/.memorytree/hub/07_reports/）

3. heartbeat 集成 — 每轮 heartbeat 结束后，如果有项目 generate_report=true，额外跑一次全局报告构建

4. /projects/index.html 自然就对了 — 因为 manifests 包含了所有项目，extractProject 按 cwd 末段分组，papaweb/memorytree-workflow/openmnemo 全部出现

### 优点
- 零新增 CSS/模板，复用全部现有渲染基础设施
- i18n、搜索、dashboard 统计都自动是全局的
- Caddy 配置逻辑完全不变
- 不引入新的 CLI 命令

---

这个方向你认可吗？确认后我立刻开始实现。

   176→export async function processProject(
   177→  config: Config,
   178→  projectPath: string,
   179→  projectName: string,
   180→  project?: ProjectEntry,
   181→): Promise<void> {
   182→  const logger = getLogger()
   183→  const repoSlug = slugify(projectName, 'project')
   184→  const globalRoot = defaultGlobalTranscriptRoot()
   185→  const branch = currentBranch(projectPath)
   186→  const mirrorToRepo = isDedicatedMemorytreeBranch(branch, project)
   187→  const autoPush = project?.auto_push ?? config.auto_push ?? true
   188→  const generateReport = project?.generate_report ?? config.generate_report ?? false
   189→  const aiSummaryModel = project?.ai_summary_model ?? config.ai_summary_model ?? 'claude-haiku-4-5-20251001'
   190→  const locale = project?.locale ?? config.locale ?? 'en'
   191→  const ghPagesBranch = project?.gh_pages_branch ?? config.gh_pages_branch ?? ''
   192→  const cname = project?.cname ?? config.cname ?? ''
   193→  const webhookUrl = project?.webhook_url ?? config.webhook_url ?? ''
   194→  const reportBaseUrl = project?.report_base_url ?? config.report_base_url ?? ''
   195→
   196→  if (!mirrorToRepo) {
   197→    logger.warn(
   198→      `[${projectName}] Current branch '${branch}' is not a dedicated MemoryTree branch. ` +
   199→      'Importing to the global archive only.',
   200→    )
   201→  }
   202→
   203→  const discovered = discoverSourceFiles()
   204→  let importedCount = 0
   205→
   206→  for (const [client, source] of discovered) {
   207→    let parsed: ParsedTranscript
   208→    try {
   209→      parsed = parseTranscript(client, source)
   210→    } catch {
   211→      logger.debug(`Failed to parse ${source}, skipping.`)
   212→      continue
   213→    }
   214→
   215→    if (!transcriptHasContent(parsed)) continue
   216→    if (!transcriptMatchesRepo(parsed, projectPath, repoSlug)) continue
   217→
   218→    scanSensitive(parsed, projectPath)
   219→
   220→    try {
   221→      await importTranscript(parsed, projectPath, globalRoot, repoSlug, 'not-set', mirrorToRepo)
   222→      importedCount++
   223→    } catch {
   224→      logger.exception(`Failed to import transcript: ${source}`)
   225→    }
   226→  }
   227→
   228→  if (importedCount === 0) {
   229→    logger.info(`[${projectName}] No new transcripts to import.`)
   230→    return
   231→  }
   232→
   233→  logger.info(`[${projectName}] Imported ${importedCount} transcript(s).`)
   234→  if (mirrorToRepo) {
   235→    gitCommitAndPush({ auto_push: autoPush }, projectPath, projectName, importedCount)
   236→  } else {
   237→    logger.info(`[${projectName}] Skipped repo-local commit/push on branch '${branch}'.`)
   238→  }
   239→
   240→  if (generateReport) {
   241→    try {
   242→      const { buildReport } = await import('../report/build.js')
   243→      await buildReport({
   244→        root: projectPath,
   245→        output: join(projectPath, 'Memory', '07_reports'),
   246→        noAi: !process.env['ANTHROPIC_API_KEY'],
   247→        model: aiSummaryModel,
   248→        locale,
   249→        ghPagesBranch,
   250→        cname,
   251→        webhookUrl,
   252→        reportBaseUrl,
   253→      })
   254→      logger.info(`[${projectName}] Report generated.`)
   255→    } catch (err: unknown) {
   256→      logger.warn(`[${projectName}] Report generation failed: ${String(err)}`)
   257→      // Never propagate — report failure must not abort heartbeat cycle
   258→    }
   259→  }
   260→}
