   261→function loadManifestsRecursive(dir: string, out: ManifestEntry[]): void {
   262→  let entries: string[]
   263→  try {
   264→    entries = readdirSync(dir)
   265→  } catch {
   266→    return
   267→  }
   268→
   269→  for (const entry of entries) {
   270→    const fullPath = join(dir, entry)
   271→    if (entry.endsWith('.json')) {
   272→      try {
   273→        const raw = readFileSync(fullPath, 'utf-8')
   274→        const parsed: unknown = JSON.parse(raw)
   275→        if (
   276→          parsed !== null &&
   277→          typeof parsed === 'object' &&
   278→          typeof (parsed as Record<string, unknown>)['session_id'] === 'string' &&
   279→          typeof (parsed as Record<string, unknown>)['client'] === 'string'
   280→        ) {
   281→          out.push(parsed as ManifestEntry)
   282→        }
   283→      } catch {
   284→        // Skip malformed manifests
   285→      }
   286→    } else {
   287→      // Recurse into subdirectories
   288→      loadManifestsRecursive(fullPath, out)
   289→    }
   290→  }
   291→}
   292→
   293→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   294→// Clean markdown message parsing
   295→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   296→
   297→/** Parse messages from a clean markdown file. */
   298→export function parseCleanMarkdownMessages(m: ManifestEntry, root: string): RenderedMessage[] {
   299→  const cleanPath = m.repo_clean_path
   300→    ? join(root, m.repo_clean_path)
   301→    : m.global_clean_path
   302→  if (!cleanPath || !existsSync(cleanPath)) return []
   303→
   304→  let content: string
   305→  try {
   306→    content = readFileSync(cleanPath, 'utf-8')
   307→  } catch {
   308→    return []
   309→  }
   310→
   311→  return parseMessagesFromMarkdown(content)
   312→}
   313→
   314→/** Extract role/timestamp/text from clean markdown format. */
   315→export function parseMessagesFromMarkdown(content: string): RenderedMessage[] {
   316→  const messages: RenderedMessage[] = []
   317→
   318→  // Find ## Messages section
   319→  const msgSection = content.indexOf('\n## Messages')
   320→  if (msgSection === -1) return []
   321→
   322→  const body = content.slice(msgSection + 12) // after "## Messages\n"
   323→
   324→  // Split on ### N. role headers
   325→  const msgRe = /^### \d+\.\s+(\w+)/gm
   326→  let match: RegExpExecArray | null
   327→  const starts: Array<{ index: number; role: string }> = []
   328→
   329→  while ((match = msgRe.exec(body)) !== null) {
   330→    starts.push({ index: match.index, role: match[1] ?? 'unknown' })
   331→  }
   332→
   333→  for (let i = 0; i < starts.length; i++) {
   334→    const start = starts[i]
   335→    if (!start) continue
   336→    const nextStart = starts[i + 1]
   337→    const chunk = nextStart
   338→      ? body.slice(start.index, nextStart.index)
   339→      : body.slice(start.index)
   340→
   341→    const lines = chunk.split('\n')
   342→    // First line is the header, second may be timestamp
   343→    let timestamp = ''
   344→    const textLines: string[] = []
   345→    let pastHeader = false
   346→
   347→    for (const line of lines) {
   348→      if (!pastHeader && line.startsWith('### ')) {
   349→        pastHeader = true
   350→        continue
   351→      }
   352→      if (!pastHeader) continue
   353→      const tsMatch = line.match(/^- Timestamp:\s*`([^`]+)`/)
   354→      if (tsMatch && !timestamp) {
   355→        timestamp = tsMatch[1] ?? ''
   356→        continue
   357→      }
   358→      textLines.push(line)
   359→    }

我现在有足够信息开始实现了。

方案总结（实施前确认）：

1. BuildReportOptions 新增 extraManifestRoots?: string[] — 额外的 manifest 目录列表
2. loadManifests 支持多个 root 合并
3. buildReport 新增 globalMode 入口函数 buildGlobalReport(options) — 读 config.toml，收集所有项目 manifest 路径，写入 ~/.memorytree/hub/07_reports/
4. heartbeat 循环结束后，若任意项目 generate_report=true，自动调用 buildGlobalReport
5. Caddy 片段改为指向 ~/.memorytree/hub/07_reports/（通过 memorytree caddy enable 重跑）

    94→export function isCaddyInstalled(): boolean {

   103→export function findManagedPortConflict(projectId: string, reportPort: number): string | null {
   104→  const { sitesDir, fragmentPath } = managedCaddyPaths(projectId)
   105→  if (!existsSync(sitesDir)) return null
   106→
   107→  for (const entry of readdirSync(sitesDir)) {
   108→    if (!entry.endsWith('.caddy')) continue
   109→    const currentPath = resolve(sitesDir, entry)
   110→    if (currentPath === fragmentPath) continue
   111→
   112→    const text = readFileSync(currentPath, 'utf-8')
   113→    const portMatch = text.match(/^# report_port:\s*(\d+)\s*$/m)
   114→    if (!portMatch) continue
   115→
   116→    const currentPort = parseInt(portMatch[1]!, 10)
   117→    if (currentPort !== reportPort) continue
   118→
   119→    const projectMatch = text.match(/^# project_id:\s*(.+)\s*$/m)
   120→    return projectMatch?.[1]?.trim() || entry.replace(/\.caddy$/i, '')
   121→  }
   122→
   123→  return null
   124→}

   126→export function enableManagedCaddy(project: ProjectEntry): ManagedCaddyEnableResult {
   127→  const paths = managedCaddyPaths(project.id)
   128→  const conflictProjectId = findManagedPortConflict(project.id, project.report_port)
   129→  if (conflictProjectId !== null) {
   130→    throw new Error(
   131→      `Port ${String(project.report_port)} is already used by another managed Caddy site (${conflictProjectId}). ` +
   132→      'Change this project\'s report_port first, then rerun the command.',
   133→    )
   134→  }
   135→
   136→  mkdirSync(paths.rootDir, { recursive: true })
   137→  mkdirSync(paths.sitesDir, { recursive: true })
   138→
   139→  const reportDir = projectReportDir(project)
   140→  mkdirSync(reportDir, { recursive: true })
   141→
   142→  writeTextIfChanged(paths.mainConfigPath, renderManagedMainCaddyfile())
   143→  writeTextIfChanged(paths.fragmentPath, renderManagedProjectFragment(project, reportDir))
   144→  validateManagedCaddyConfig(paths.mainConfigPath)
   145→  try {
   146→    reloadManagedCaddy(paths.mainConfigPath)
   147→  } catch (error: unknown) {
   148→    throw new Error(
   149→      `Caddy config files were updated, but reload failed. ${formatExecError(error)} ` +
   150→      `Start Caddy with: ${managedCaddyStartCommand()}`,
   151→    )
   152→  }
   153→
   154→  return {
   155→    mainConfigPath: paths.mainConfigPath,
   156→    fragmentPath: paths.fragmentPath,
   157→    reportDir,
   158→    localUrls: localUrlsForProject(project.report_port),
   159→    lanUrls: lanUrlsForProject(project.report_port, project.report_exposure),
   160→  }
   161→}

   163→export function disableManagedCaddy(project: Pick<ProjectEntry, 'id' | 'report_port' | 'report_exposure'>): ManagedCaddyEnableResult {
   164→  const paths = managedCaddyPaths(project.id)
   165→  if (existsSync(paths.fragmentPath)) {
   166→    rmSync(paths.fragmentPath, { force: true })
   167→  }
   168→
   169→  if (existsSync(paths.mainConfigPath)) {
   170→    validateManagedCaddyConfig(paths.mainConfigPath)
   171→    try {
   172→      reloadManagedCaddy(paths.mainConfigPath)
   173→    } catch (error: unknown) {
   174→      throw new Error(
   175→        `The project fragment was removed, but Caddy reload failed. ${formatExecError(error)} ` +
   176→        `Start Caddy with: ${managedCaddyStartCommand()}`,
   177→      )
   178→    }
   179→  }
   180→
   181→  return {
   182→    mainConfigPath: paths.mainConfigPath,
   183→    fragmentPath: paths.fragmentPath,
   184→    reportDir: '',
   185→    localUrls: localUrlsForProject(project.report_port),
   186→    lanUrls: lanUrlsForProject(project.report_port, project.report_exposure),
   187→  }
   188→}

   190→export async function loadManagedCaddyStatus(project: ProjectEntry): Promise<ManagedCaddyStatus> {
   191→  const paths = managedCaddyPaths(project.id)
   192→  const installed = isCaddyInstalled()
   193→  const mainConfigExists = existsSync(paths.mainConfigPath)
   194→  const fragmentExists = existsSync(paths.fragmentPath)
   195→  const runningConfigText = installed ? await fetchRunningCaddyConfigText() : null
   196→  const running = runningConfigText !== null
   197→
   198→  let usingManagedConfig: boolean | null = null
   199→  if (installed && running && mainConfigExists) {
   200→    const managedConfigText = adaptManagedCaddyConfig(paths.mainConfigPath)
   201→    usingManagedConfig = stableJsonFromText(managedConfigText) === stableJsonFromText(runningConfigText)
   202→  }
   203→
   204→  return {
   205→    installed,
   206→    running,
   207→    usingManagedConfig,
   208→    mainConfigPath: paths.mainConfigPath,
   209→    mainConfigExists,
   210→    fragmentPath: paths.fragmentPath,

   268→function stableJsonFromText(text: string | null): string | null {
   269→  if (text === null) return null
   270→  try {
   271→    return JSON.stringify(sortJsonKeys(JSON.parse(text)))
   272→  } catch {
   273→    return null
   274→  }
   275→}
   276→
   277→function sortJsonKeys(value: unknown): unknown {
   278→  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
   279→    return value.map(item => sortJsonKeys(item))
   280→  }
   281→  if (value !== null && typeof value === 'object') {
   282→    return Object.fromEntries(
   283→      Object.keys(value)
   284→        .sort((left, right) => left.localeCompare(right))
   285→        .map(key => [key, sortJsonKeys((value as Record<string, unknown>)[key])]),
   286→    )
   287→  }
   288→  return value
   289→}

   291→function localUrlsForProject(reportPort: number): string[] {
   292→  return [
   293→    `http://127.0.0.1:${String(reportPort)}/`,

   297→
   298→function lanUrlsForProject(
   299→  reportPort: number,
   300→  exposure: ProjectEntry['report_exposure'],
   301→): string[] {
   302→  if (exposure !== 'lan') return []
   303→
   304→  const urls = new Set<string>()
   305→  const interfaces = networkInterfaces()
   306→  for (const addresses of Object.values(interfaces)) {
   307→    for (const address of addresses ?? []) {
   308→      if (address.family !== 'IPv4' || address.internal) continue
   309→      urls.add(`http://${address.address}:${String(reportPort)}/`)
   310→    }
   311→  }
   312→  return [...urls].sort((left, right) => left.localeCompare(right))
   313→}

   315→function formatExecError(error: unknown): string {
   316→  if (error instanceof Error && error.message) {
   317→    return error.message
   318→  }
   319→  return String(error)
   320→}

   106→export function loadConfig(): Config {
   107→  const path = configPath()
   108→  if (!existsSync(path)) {
   109→    return defaultConfig()
   110→  }
   111→
   112→  let raw: Record<string, unknown>
   113→  try {
   114→    const text = readFileSync(path, 'utf-8')
   115→    raw = parseToml(text) as Record<string, unknown>
   116→  } catch {
   117→    return defaultConfig()
   118→  }
   119→
   120→  return parseRaw(raw)
   121→}

   183→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   184→// Interval parsing
   185→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   186→
   187→export function intervalToSeconds(interval: string): number {
   188→  const match = interval.trim().toLowerCase().match(/^(\d+)\s*(s|m|h)$/)
   189→  if (!match) {
   190→    return intervalToSeconds(DEFAULT_HEARTBEAT_INTERVAL)
   191→  }
   192→  const value = parseInt(match[1]!, 10)
   193→  const unit = match[2]!
   194→  if (value <= 0) {
   195→    return intervalToSeconds(DEFAULT_HEARTBEAT_INTERVAL)
   196→  }
   197→  const multiplier: Record<string, number> = { s: 1, m: 60, h: 3600 }
   198→  return value * (multiplier[unit] ?? 60)
   199→}

   205→export function registerProject(
   206→  cfg: Config,
   207→  repoPath: string,
   208→  overrides: Partial<ProjectLike> = {},
   209→): Config {
   210→  const normalized = normalizeConfig(cfg)
   211→  const resolved = normalizePath(repoPath)
   212→  for (const entry of normalized.projects) {
   213→    if (projectContainsPath(entry, resolved)) {
   214→      return normalized
   215→    }
   216→  }
   217→
   218→  const projectInput: Record<string, unknown> = {
   219→    path: overrides.path ?? resolved,
   220→    development_path: overrides.development_path ?? resolved,
   221→    memory_path: overrides.memory_path ?? resolved,
   222→  }
   223→  if (overrides.name !== undefined) projectInput.name = overrides.name
   224→  if (overrides.id !== undefined) projectInput.id = overrides.id
   225→  if (overrides.heartbeat_interval !== undefined) projectInput.heartbeat_interval = overrides.heartbeat_interval
   226→  if (overrides.refresh_interval !== undefined) projectInput.refresh_interval = overrides.refresh_interval
   227→  if (overrides.memory_branch !== undefined) projectInput.memory_branch = overrides.memory_branch
   228→  if (overrides.auto_push !== undefined) projectInput.auto_push = overrides.auto_push
   229→  if (overrides.generate_report !== undefined) projectInput.generate_report = overrides.generate_report
   230→  if (overrides.ai_summary_model !== undefined) projectInput.ai_summary_model = overrides.ai_summary_model
   231→  if (overrides.locale !== undefined) projectInput.locale = overrides.locale
   232→  if (overrides.gh_pages_branch !== undefined) projectInput.gh_pages_branch = overrides.gh_pages_branch
   233→  if (overrides.cname !== undefined) projectInput.cname = overrides.cname
   234→  if (overrides.webhook_url !== undefined) projectInput.webhook_url = overrides.webhook_url
   235→  if (overrides.report_base_url !== undefined) projectInput.report_base_url = overrides.report_base_url
   236→  if (overrides.report_port !== undefined) projectInput.report_port = overrides.report_port
   237→  if (overrides.report_exposure !== undefined) projectInput.report_exposure = overrides.report_exposure
   238→  if (overrides.last_heartbeat_at !== undefined) projectInput.last_heartbeat_at = overrides.last_heartbeat_at
   239→
   240→  const project = normalizeProjectEntry(projectInput as ProjectLike, normalized)
   241→
   242→  return {
   243→    ...normalized,
   244→    projects: [...normalized.projects, project],
   245→  }
   246→}

   248→export function upsertProject(
   249→  cfg: Config,
   250→  repoPath: string,
   251→  overrides: Partial<ProjectLike> = {},
   252→): Config {
   253→  const normalized = normalizeConfig(cfg)
   254→  const resolved = normalizePath(repoPath)
   255→  const existing = findProjectForPath(normalized, resolved)
   256→  if (existing === null) {
   257→    return registerProject(normalized, repoPath, overrides)
   258→  }
   259→
   260→  const project = normalizeProjectEntry({
   261→    ...existing,
   262→    ...overrides,
   263→    development_path: overrides.development_path ?? existing.development_path,
   264→    memory_path: overrides.memory_path ?? existing.memory_path,
   265→    memory_branch: overrides.memory_branch ?? existing.memory_branch,
   266→    path: overrides.path ?? existing.path,
   267→  }, normalized)
   268→
   269→  return {
   270→    ...normalized,
   271→    projects: normalized.projects.map(entry => (
   272→      entry.id === existing.id ? project : entry
   273→    )),
   274→  }
   275→}

   277→export function findProjectForPath(config: Config, candidatePath: string): ProjectEntry | null {
   278→  const normalized = normalizePath(candidatePath)
   279→  let bestMatch: ProjectEntry | null = null
   280→  let bestLength = -1
   281→
   282→  for (const entry of config.projects) {
   283→    for (const root of projectRoots(entry)) {
   284→      if (!pathContains(root, normalized)) continue
   285→      if (root.length > bestLength) {
   286→        bestMatch = entry
   287→        bestLength = root.length
   288→      }
   289→    }
   290→  }
   291→
   292→  return bestMatch
   293→}

   313→export function projectIsDue(project: ProjectEntry, now: Date = new Date()): boolean {
   314→  if (!project.last_heartbeat_at) return true
   315→
   316→  const lastRunMs = Date.parse(project.last_heartbeat_at)
   317→  if (!Number.isFinite(lastRunMs)) return true
   318→
   319→  const dueAfterMs = intervalToSeconds(project.heartbeat_interval) * 1000
   320→  return now.getTime() - lastRunMs >= dueAfterMs
   321→}
   322→
   323→export function projectRefreshIsDue(project: ProjectEntry, now: Date = new Date()): boolean {
   324→  if (!project.last_refresh_at) return true
   325→
   326→  const lastRefreshMs = Date.parse(project.last_refresh_at)
   327→  if (!Number.isFinite(lastRefreshMs)) return true
   328→
   329→  const dueAfterMs = intervalToSeconds(project.refresh_interval) * 1000
   330→  return now.getTime() - lastRefreshMs >= dueAfterMs
   331→}

   380→function parseRaw(raw: Record<string, unknown>): Config {
   381→  const interval = typeof raw['heartbeat_interval'] === 'string' && isValidInterval(raw['heartbeat_interval'])
   382→    ? raw['heartbeat_interval']
   383→    : DEFAULT_HEARTBEAT_INTERVAL
   384→
   385→  const autoPush = typeof raw['auto_push'] === 'boolean'
   386→    ? raw['auto_push']
   387→    : DEFAULT_AUTO_PUSH
   388→
   389→  const rawLogLevel = raw['log_level']
   390→  const logLevel = typeof rawLogLevel === 'string' && VALID_LOG_LEVELS.has(rawLogLevel.toLowerCase())
   391→    ? rawLogLevel.toLowerCase()
   392→    : DEFAULT_LOG_LEVEL
   393→
   394→  const watchDirs: string[] = []
   395→  const rawDirs = raw['watch_dirs']
   396→  if (Array.isArray(rawDirs)) {
   397→    for (const dir of rawDirs) {
   398→      if (typeof dir === 'string') {
   399→        watchDirs.push(dir)
   400→      }
   401→    }
   402→  }
   403→
   404→  const generateReport = typeof raw['generate_report'] === 'boolean'
   405→    ? raw['generate_report']
   406→    : DEFAULT_GENERATE_REPORT
   407→
   408→  const aiSummaryModel = typeof raw['ai_summary_model'] === 'string' && raw['ai_summary_model']
   409→    ? raw['ai_summary_model']
   410→    : DEFAULT_AI_SUMMARY_MODEL
   411→
   412→  const locale = typeof raw['locale'] === 'string' && raw['locale']
   413→    ? raw['locale']
   414→    : DEFAULT_LOCALE
   415→
   416→  const ghPagesBranch = typeof raw['gh_pages_branch'] === 'string'
   417→    ? raw['gh_pages_branch']
   418→    : DEFAULT_GH_PAGES_BRANCH
   419→
   420→  const cname = typeof raw['cname'] === 'string'
   421→    ? raw['cname']
   422→    : DEFAULT_CNAME
   423→
   424→  const webhookUrl = typeof raw['webhook_url'] === 'string'
   425→    ? raw['webhook_url']
   426→    : DEFAULT_WEBHOOK_URL
   427→
   428→  const reportBaseUrl = typeof raw['report_base_url'] === 'string'
   429→    ? raw['report_base_url']
   430→    : DEFAULT_REPORT_BASE_URL
   431→
   432→  const reportPort = isValidPort(raw['report_port'])
   433→    ? raw['report_port']
   434→    : DEFAULT_REPORT_PORT
   435→  const reportExposure = normalizeReportExposure(raw['report_exposure'], DEFAULT_REPORT_EXPOSURE)
   436→
   437→  const cfg: Config = {
   438→    heartbeat_interval: interval,
   439→    watch_dirs: watchDirs,
   440→    projects: [],
   441→    auto_push: autoPush,
   442→    log_level: logLevel,
   443→    generate_report: generateReport,
   444→    ai_summary_model: aiSummaryModel,
   445→    locale,
   446→    gh_pages_branch: ghPagesBranch,
   447→    cname,
   448→    webhook_url: webhookUrl,
   449→    report_base_url: reportBaseUrl,
   450→    report_port: reportPort,
   451→    report_exposure: reportExposure,
   452→  }
   453→
   454→  const projects: ProjectEntry[] = []
   455→  const rawProjects = raw['projects']
   456→  if (Array.isArray(rawProjects)) {
   457→    for (const entry of rawProjects) {
   458→      if (entry === null || typeof entry !== 'object' || Array.isArray(entry)) continue
   459→      try {
   460→        const normalized = normalizeProjectEntry(entry as ProjectLike, cfg)
   461→        projects.push(normalized)
   462→      } catch {
   463→        continue
   464→      }
   465→    }
   466→  }
   467→
   468→  return {
   469→    ...cfg,
   470→    projects,
   471→  }
   472→}
   473→
   474→function normalizeConfig(cfg: Config): Config {
   475→  const normalizedBase: Config = {
   476→    heartbeat_interval: isValidInterval(cfg.heartbeat_interval) ? cfg.heartbeat_interval : DEFAULT_HEARTBEAT_INTERVAL,
   477→    watch_dirs: [...cfg.watch_dirs].filter((dir): dir is string => typeof dir === 'string'),
   478→    projects: [],
   479→    auto_push: typeof cfg.auto_push === 'boolean' ? cfg.auto_push : DEFAULT_AUTO_PUSH,
   480→    log_level: isValidLogLevel(cfg.log_level) ? cfg.log_level.toLowerCase() : DEFAULT_LOG_LEVEL,
   481→    generate_report: typeof cfg.generate_report === 'boolean' ? cfg.generate_report : DEFAULT_GENERATE_REPORT,
   482→    ai_summary_model: nonEmptyString(cfg.ai_summary_model, DEFAULT_AI_SUMMARY_MODEL),
   483→    locale: nonEmptyString(cfg.locale, DEFAULT_LOCALE),
   484→    gh_pages_branch: stringOrDefault(cfg.gh_pages_branch, DEFAULT_GH_PAGES_BRANCH),
   485→    cname: stringOrDefault(cfg.cname, DEFAULT_CNAME),
   486→    webhook_url: stringOrDefault(cfg.webhook_url, DEFAULT_WEBHOOK_URL),
   487→    report_base_url: stringOrDefault(cfg.report_base_url, DEFAULT_REPORT_BASE_URL),
   488→    report_port: isValidPort(cfg.report_port) ? cfg.report_port : DEFAULT_REPORT_PORT,
   489→    report_exposure: normalizeReportExposure(cfg.report_exposure, DEFAULT_REPORT_EXPOSURE),
   490→  }
   491→
   492→  const projects = cfg.projects.map(project => normalizeProjectEntry(project, normalizedBase))
   493→  return {
   494→    ...normalizedBase,
   495→    projects,
   496→  }
   497→}
   498→
   499→function normalizeProjectEntry(project: ProjectLike, cfg: Config): ProjectEntry {
   500→  const rawPath = maybeNormalizePath(project.path)
   501→  const developmentPath = maybeNormalizePath(project.development_path) || rawPath
   502→  const memoryPath = maybeNormalizePath(project.memory_path) || rawPath || developmentPath
   503→  const canonicalPath = memoryPath || rawPath || developmentPath
   504→
   505→  if (!canonicalPath) {
   506→    throw new Error('Project entry requires at least one path.')
   507→  }
   508→
   509→  const resolvedDevelopmentPath = developmentPath || canonicalPath
   510→  const resolvedMemoryPath = memoryPath || canonicalPath
   511→  const name = nonEmptyString(project.name, basename(resolvedDevelopmentPath))
   512→  const id = createProjectId(
   513→    typeof project.id === 'string' ? project.id : '',
   514→    resolvedDevelopmentPath,
   515→    resolvedMemoryPath,
   516→  )
   517→
   518→  return {
   519→    id,
   520→    path: canonicalPath,
   521→    name,
   522→    development_path: resolvedDevelopmentPath,
   523→    memory_path: resolvedMemoryPath,
   524→    memory_branch: nonEmptyString(project.memory_branch, DEFAULT_MEMORY_BRANCH),
   525→    heartbeat_interval: isValidInterval(project.heartbeat_interval ?? '') ? project.heartbeat_interval! : cfg.heartbeat_interval,
   526→    refresh_interval: isValidInterval(project.refresh_interval ?? '') ? project.refresh_interval! : DEFAULT_REFRESH_INTERVAL,
   527→    auto_push: typeof project.auto_push === 'boolean' ? project.auto_push : cfg.auto_push,
   528→    generate_report: typeof project.generate_report === 'boolean' ? project.generate_report : cfg.generate_report,
   529→    ai_summary_model: nonEmptyString(project.ai_summary_model, cfg.ai_summary_model),
   530→    locale: nonEmptyString(project.locale, cfg.locale),
   531→    gh_pages_branch: stringOrDefault(project.gh_pages_branch, cfg.gh_pages_branch),
   532→    cname: stringOrDefault(project.cname, cfg.cname),
   533→    webhook_url: stringOrDefault(project.webhook_url, cfg.webhook_url),
   534→    report_base_url: stringOrDefault(project.report_base_url, cfg.report_base_url),
   535→    report_port: isValidPort(project.report_port) ? project.report_port : cfg.report_port,
   536→    report_exposure: normalizeReportExposure(project.report_exposure, cfg.report_exposure),
   537→    last_heartbeat_at: isValidIsoTimestamp(project.last_heartbeat_at) ? project.last_heartbeat_at : '',
   538→    last_refresh_at: isValidIsoTimestamp(project.last_refresh_at) ? project.last_refresh_at : '',
   539→  }
   540→}
   541→
   542→function isValidInterval(value: string): boolean {
   543→  const match = value.trim().toLowerCase().match(/^(\d+)\s*(s|m|h)$/)
   544→  if (!match) return false
   545→  return parseInt(match[1]!, 10) > 0
   546→}
   547→
   548→function isValidPort(value: unknown): value is number {
   549→  return typeof value === 'number'
   550→    && Number.isInteger(value)
   551→    && value > 0
   552→    && value <= 65535
   553→}
   554→
   555→function normalizeReportExposure(value: unknown, fallback: ReportExposure): ReportExposure {
   556→  if (typeof value !== 'string') return fallback
   557→  const normalized = value.trim().toLowerCase()
   558→  return normalized === 'lan' ? 'lan' : normalized === 'local' ? 'local' : fallback
   559→}
   560→
   561→function isValidIsoTimestamp(value: unknown): value is string {
   562→  return typeof value === 'string'
   563→    && value.length > 0
   564→    && Number.isFinite(Date.parse(value))
   565→}
   566→
   567→function isValidLogLevel(value: unknown): value is string {
   568→  return typeof value === 'string' && VALID_LOG_LEVELS.has(value.toLowerCase())
   569→}
   570→
   571→function nonEmptyString(value: unknown, fallback: string): string {
   572→  return typeof value === 'string' && value ? value : fallback
   573→}
   574→
   575→function stringOrDefault(value: unknown, fallback: string): string {
   576→  return typeof value === 'string' ? value : fallback
   577→}
   578→
   579→function maybeNormalizePath(value: unknown): string {
   580→  return typeof value === 'string' && value
   581→    ? normalizePath(value)
   582→    : ''
   583→}
   584→
   585→function normalizePath(value: string): string {
   586→  if (value.startsWith('/')) {
   587→    return toPosixPath(value)
   588→  }
   589→  if (/^[a-zA-Z]:[\\/]/.test(value) || value.startsWith('\\\\')) {
   590→    return toPosixPath(resolve(value))
   591→  }
   592→  return toPosixPath(resolve(value))
   593→}
   594→
   595→function createProjectId(requestedId: string, developmentPath: string, memoryPath: string): string {
   596→  const source = requestedId || `${developmentPath}--${memoryPath}`
   597→  const normalized = source
   598→    .toLowerCase()
   599→    .replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, '-')
   600→    .replace(/^-+|-+$/g, '')
   601→    .replace(/-{2,}/g, '-')
   602→
   603→  return normalized || 'project'
   604→}
   605→
   606→function projectRoots(project: ProjectEntry): string[] {
   607→  return [...new Set([
   608→    normalizePath(project.development_path),
   609→    normalizePath(project.memory_path),
   610→    normalizePath(project.path),
   611→  ])]
   612→}
   613→
   614→function projectContainsPath(project: ProjectEntry, candidatePath: string): boolean {
   615→  return projectRoots(project).some(root => pathContains(root, candidatePath))
   616→}
   617→
   618→function pathContains(root: string, candidate: string): boolean {
   619→  if (candidate === root) return true
   620→  const prefix = root.endsWith('/') ? root : `${root}/`
   621→  return candidate.startsWith(prefix)
   622→}
   623→
   624→function tomlString(value: string): string {
   625→  const escaped = value.replace(/\\/g, '\\\\').replace(/"/g, '\\"')
   626→  return `"${escaped}"`
   627→}

    94→export function isCaddyInstalled(): boolean {

   103→export function findManagedPortConflict(projectId: string, reportPort: number): string | null {
   104→  const { sitesDir, fragmentPath } = managedCaddyPaths(projectId)
   105→  if (!existsSync(sitesDir)) return null
   106→
   107→  for (const entry of readdirSync(sitesDir)) {
   108→    if (!entry.endsWith('.caddy')) continue
   109→    const currentPath = resolve(sitesDir, entry)
   110→    if (currentPath === fragmentPath) continue
   111→
   112→    const text = readFileSync(currentPath, 'utf-8')
   113→    const portMatch = text.match(/^# report_port:\s*(\d+)\s*$/m)
   114→    if (!portMatch) continue
   115→
   116→    const currentPort = parseInt(portMatch[1]!, 10)
   117→    if (currentPort !== reportPort) continue
   118→
   119→    const projectMatch = text.match(/^# project_id:\s*(.+)\s*$/m)
   120→    return projectMatch?.[1]?.trim() || entry.replace(/\.caddy$/i, '')
   121→  }
   122→
   123→  return null
   124→}
   125→
   126→export function enableManagedCaddy(project: ProjectEntry): ManagedCaddyEnableResult {
   127→  const paths = managedCaddyPaths(project.id)
   128→  const conflictProjectId = findManagedPortConflict(project.id, project.report_port)
   129→  if (conflictProjectId !== null) {
   130→    throw new Error(
   131→      `Port ${String(project.report_port)} is already used by another managed Caddy site (${conflictProjectId}). ` +
   132→      'Change this project\'s report_port first, then rerun the command.',
   133→    )
   134→  }
   135→
   136→  mkdirSync(paths.rootDir, { recursive: true })
   137→  mkdirSync(paths.sitesDir, { recursive: true })
   138→
   139→  const reportDir = projectReportDir(project)
   140→  mkdirSync(reportDir, { recursive: true })
   141→
   142→  writeTextIfChanged(paths.mainConfigPath, renderManagedMainCaddyfile())
   143→  writeTextIfChanged(paths.fragmentPath, renderManagedProjectFragment(project, reportDir))
   144→  validateManagedCaddyConfig(paths.mainConfigPath)
   145→  try {
   146→    reloadManagedCaddy(paths.mainConfigPath)
   147→  } catch (error: unknown) {
   148→    throw new Error(
   149→      `Caddy config files were updated, but reload failed. ${formatExecError(error)} ` +
   150→      `Start Caddy with: ${managedCaddyStartCommand()}`,
   151→    )
   152→  }
   153→
   154→  return {
   155→    mainConfigPath: paths.mainConfigPath,
   156→    fragmentPath: paths.fragmentPath,
   157→    reportDir,
   158→    localUrls: localUrlsForProject(project.report_port),
   159→    lanUrls: lanUrlsForProject(project.report_port, project.report_exposure),
   160→  }
   161→}

    22→export function renderProjects(manifests: ManifestEntry[], t?: Translations): string {
    23→  const nav = renderNav('projects', 1, t)
    24→  const title = t?.projects.title ?? 'Projects'
    25→
    26→  if (manifests.length === 0) {
    27→    const content = `<div class="page-header">
    28→  <h1>${escHtml(title)}</h1>
    29→  <p class="subtitle">${escHtml(t?.projects.noProjects ?? 'No projects found.')}</p>
    30→</div>`
    31→    return htmlShell(title, content, nav)
    32→  }
    33→
    34→  // Group by project name
    35→  const projectMap = new Map<string, ManifestEntry[]>()
    36→  for (const m of manifests) {
    37→    const proj = extractProject(m.cwd)
    38→    const group = projectMap.get(proj)
    39→    if (group) {
    40→      group.push(m)
    41→    } else {
    42→      projectMap.set(proj, [m])
    43→    }
    44→  }
    45→
    46→  // Sort by session count desc
    47→  const sorted = [...projectMap.entries()].sort((a, b) => b[1].length - a[1].length)
    48→
    49→  const sessionLabel = t?.projects.sessions ?? 'sessions'
    50→
    51→  const cards = sorted.map(([name, sessions]) => {
    52→    const count = sessions.length
    53→    const lastActive = sessions
    54→      .map(s => s.started_at)
    55→      .sort()
    56→      .at(-1)
    57→      ?.slice(0, 10) ?? '—'
    58→
    59→    const clients = [...new Set(sessions.map(s => s.client))]
    60→    const badges = clients.map(c => clientBadge(c)).join(' ')
    61→
    62→    return `<div class="project-card">
    63→  <div class="project-card-name">${escHtml(name)}</div>
    64→  <div class="project-card-meta">
    65→    ${count} ${escHtml(sessionLabel)} · last active ${escHtml(lastActive)}
    66→  </div>
    67→  <div class="project-card-clients">${badges}</div>
    68→</div>`
    69→  }).join('\n')
    70→
    71→  const content = `<div class="page-header">
    72→  <h1>${escHtml(title)}</h1>
    73→  <p class="subtitle">${sorted.length} project(s)</p>
    74→</div>
    75→<div class="project-grid">
    76→${cards}
    77→</div>`
    78→
    79→  return htmlShell(title, content, nav)
    80→}

    63→export async function main(options: HeartbeatRunOptions = {}): Promise<number> {
    64→  const config = loadConfig()
    65→  setupLogging(config.log_level as LogLevel)
    66→  const logger = getLogger()
    67→
    68→  if (!acquireLock()) {
    69→    logger.info('Another heartbeat instance is running. Exiting.')
    70→    writeAlert('global', 'lock_held', 'Heartbeat exited: another instance held the lock.')
    71→    return 0
    72→  }
    73→
    74→  try {
    75→    return await runHeartbeat(config, options)
    76→  } finally {
    77→    releaseLock()
    78→  }
    79→}
    80→

    85→export async function runHeartbeat(config: Config, options: HeartbeatRunOptions = {}): Promise<number> {
    86→  const logger = getLogger()
    87→  const targetProject = options.root ? findProjectForPath(config, resolve(options.root)) : null
    88→
    89→  if (config.projects.length === 0) {
    90→    logger.info('No projects registered in config.toml. Nothing to do.')
    91→    return 0
    92→  }
    93→  if (options.root && !targetProject) {
    94→    logger.warn(`No registered project matched: ${resolve(options.root)}`)
    95→    return 1
    96→  }
    97→
    98→  const projects = targetProject ? [targetProject] : config.projects
    99→
   100→  logger.info(`Heartbeat started. ${projects.length} project(s) selected.`)

   143→      if (heartbeatDue || refreshDue) {
   144→        const outputSync = syncProjectOutputsToDevelopment(entry)
   145→        if (!outputSync.skipped) {
   146→          logger.info(
   147→            `[${projectName}] Synced outputs back to development directory ` +
   148→            `(copied ${outputSync.copied}, deleted ${outputSync.deleted}).`,
   149→          )
   150→        }
   151→        nextConfig = noteProjectRefreshRun(nextConfig, entry.id, runTimestamp)
   152→        configChanged = true
   153→      }
   154→    } catch (err: unknown) {
   155→      logger.exception(`Error processing project: ${projectPath}`, err)
   156→      writeAlertWithThreshold(
   157→        toPosixPath(projectPath),
   158→        'push_failed',
   159→        `Heartbeat error for project: ${basename(projectPath)}`,
   160→      )
   161→    }
   162→  }
   163→
   164→  if (configChanged) {
   165→    saveConfig(nextConfig)
   166→  }
   167→
   168→  logger.info('Heartbeat finished.')
   169→  return 0
   170→}

    70→  reportDir: string,

    89→  lines.push('}')

    94→export function isCaddyInstalled(): boolean {

   103→export function findManagedPortConflict(projectId: string, reportPort: number): string | null {
   104→  const { sitesDir, fragmentPath } = managedCaddyPaths(projectId)
   105→  if (!existsSync(sitesDir)) return null
   106→
   107→  for (const entry of readdirSync(sitesDir)) {
   108→    if (!entry.endsWith('.caddy')) continue
   109→    const currentPath = resolve(sitesDir, entry)
   110→    if (currentPath === fragmentPath) continue
   111→
   112→    const text = readFileSync(currentPath, 'utf-8')
   113→    const portMatch = text.match(/^# report_port:\s*(\d+)\s*$/m)
   114→    if (!portMatch) continue
   115→
   116→    const currentPort = parseInt(portMatch[1]!, 10)
   117→    if (currentPort !== reportPort) continue
   118→
   119→    const projectMatch = text.match(/^# project_id:\s*(.+)\s*$/m)
   120→    return projectMatch?.[1]?.trim() || entry.replace(/\.caddy$/i, '')
   121→  }
   122→
   123→  return null
   124→}
   125→
   126→export function enableManagedCaddy(project: ProjectEntry): ManagedCaddyEnableResult {
   127→  const paths = managedCaddyPaths(project.id)
   128→  const conflictProjectId = findManagedPortConflict(project.id, project.report_port)
   129→  if (conflictProjectId !== null) {
   130→    throw new Error(
   131→      `Port ${String(project.report_port)} is already used by another managed Caddy site (${conflictProjectId}). ` +
   132→      'Change this project\'s report_port first, then rerun the command.',
   133→    )
   134→  }

   262→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   263→// Sensitive pattern scanning
   264→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   265→
   266→export function scanSensitive(parsed: ParsedTranscript, projectPath: string): void {
   267→  const logger = getLogger()
   268→  for (const msg of parsed.messages) {
   269→    for (const pattern of SENSITIVE_PATTERNS) {
   270→      if (pattern.test(msg.text)) {
   271→        logger.warn(
   272→          `Sensitive pattern detected in transcript ${parsed.source_path} (project: ${basename(projectPath)}, role: ${msg.role})`,
   273→        )
   274→        writeAlert(
   275→          toPosixPath(projectPath),
   276→          'sensitive_match',
   277→          `Sensitive pattern in transcript: ${basename(parsed.source_path)}`,
   278→        )
   279→        return
   280→      }
   281→    }
   282→  }
   283→}

    12→export async function cmdCaddyEnable(options: { root: string }): Promise<number> {

    17→    )

    35→      process.stdout.write(`Local URL: ${url}\n`)

    39→    }
    40→    return 0

    47→export async function cmdCaddyDisable(options: { root: string }): Promise<number> {

    73→export async function cmdCaddyStatus(options: { root: string }): Promise<number> {
    74→  const project = resolveProject(options.root)
    75→  if (project === null) {
    76→    process.stderr.write(
    77→      'Project not found in ~/.memorytree/config.toml. Run `memorytree daemon quick-start --root .` first.\n',
    78→    )
    79→    return 1
    80→  }
    81→
    82→  const status = await loadManagedCaddyStatus(project)
    83→  process.stdout.write(`Caddy installed: ${yesNo(status.installed)}\n`)
    84→  process.stdout.write(`Caddy running: ${yesNo(status.running)}\n`)
    85→  process.stdout.write(`Using MemoryTree Caddyfile: ${yesNoOrUnknown(status.usingManagedConfig)}\n`)
    86→  process.stdout.write(`Project registered: ${yesNo(status.fragmentExists)}\n`)
    87→  process.stdout.write(`Port: ${String(status.port)}\n`)
    88→  process.stdout.write(`Exposure: ${status.exposure}\n`)
    89→  process.stdout.write(`Report directory: ${status.reportDir}\n`)
    90→  process.stdout.write(`Main config: ${status.mainConfigPath}\n`)
    91→  process.stdout.write(`Project fragment: ${status.fragmentPath}\n`)
    92→  for (const url of status.localUrls) {
    93→    process.stdout.write(`Local URL: ${url}\n`)
    94→  }
    95→  for (const url of status.lanUrls) {
    96→    process.stdout.write(`LAN URL: ${url}\n`)
    97→  }
    98→  if (!status.installed || !status.running || status.usingManagedConfig !== true) {
    99→    process.stdout.write(`Managed start command: ${managedCaddyStartCommand()}\n`)
   100→  }
   101→  return 0
   102→}

   104→function resolveProject(root: string): ProjectEntry | null {
   105→  const config = loadConfig()
   106→  return findProjectForPath(config, resolve(root))
   107→}
   108→
   109→function yesNo(value: boolean): string {
   110→  return value ? 'yes' : 'no'
   111→}
   112→
   113→function yesNoOrUnknown(value: boolean | null): string {
   114→  if (value === null) return 'unknown'
   115→  return yesNo(value)
   116→}
   117→
   118→function formatError(error: unknown): string {
   119→  if (error instanceof Error && error.message) {

   121→  }

    35→export function inferClient(client: string, sourcePath: string): Client {
    36→  if (client !== 'auto') {
    37→    return client as Client
    38→  }

    40→  const fileName = basename(sourcePath).toLowerCase()
    41→  if (normalized.includes('/.codex/') || fileName.startsWith('rollout-')) {
    42→    return 'codex'
    43→  }
    44→  if (normalized.includes('/.claude/') || normalized.includes('/projects/')) {
    45→    return 'claude'
    46→  }
    47→  if (normalized.includes('/.gemini/') || normalized.includes('checkpoint')) {
    48→    return 'gemini'
    49→  }
    50→  if (fileName.startsWith('doubao_') || normalized.includes('/doubao/')) {
    51→    return 'doubao'
    52→  }
    53→  throw new Error(`could not infer transcript client from source path: ${sourcePath}`)
    54→}

   112→    snippets[m.session_id] = firstMsg ? firstMsg.text.slice(0, 300) : ''
   113→

   115→    const manifest = m
   116→    const msgs = messages
   117→    summaryPromises.push(
   118→      (async () => {
   119→        try {
   120→        const summary = await getSummary(manifest.raw_sha256, msgs, summaryOptions)
   121→        summaries[manifest.session_id] = summary
   122→        const backlinkIds = linkGraph.backlinks[manifest.session_id] ?? []
   123→        const backlinkManifests = backlinkIds
   124→          .map(id => manifests.find(x => x.session_id === id))
   125→          .filter((x): x is ManifestEntry => x !== undefined)
   126→
   127→        const html = renderTranscript(msgs, manifest, summary, backlinkManifests, t, reportBaseUrl)
   128→        const outPath = transcriptOutputPath(output, manifest)
   129→        mkdirSync(dirname(outPath), { recursive: true })

   132→          // eslint-disable-next-line no-console

   135→      })(),

assistant #143 10:16:29

已经读得足够清楚了。让我向你说明分析结论，然后开始实现。

---

问题根因

buildReport 的 loadManifests(root) 只读当前项目的 Memory/06_transcripts/manifests/，所以 projects/index.html 永远只显示当前项目的会话。

最合理的方案（比我之前说的更简单）

不需要新 hub 端口、不需要新 Caddy 片段、不需要重构 Caddy 路由。

只做一件事：当 heartbeat 触发 buildReport 时，把所有已注册项目的 manifest 路径一起传进去。

memorytree-workflow 的 Memory/07_reports/ 就自然成为"机器级全局报告"，10010 就是全局 hub，Projects 页显示所有项目，Dashboard 显示所有会话数据。

改动清单：
1. BuildReportOptions 新增 extraManifestRoots?: string[]
2. build.ts 的 loadManifests 调用合并多个 root 的结果
3. heartbeat.ts 的 buildReport 调用传入其他项目的 manifest 路径

三个文件，外科手术式改动，开始：

   261→function loadManifestsRecursive(dir: string, out: ManifestEntry[]): void {
   262→  let entries: string[]
   263→  try {
   264→    entries = readdirSync(dir)
   265→  } catch {
   266→    return
   267→  }

   269→  for (const entry of entries) {

<thinking>
Now I have a complete understanding. Let me figure out the exact changes needed:

The problem: loadManifests(root) only reads from root/Memory/06_transcripts/manifests/. When heartbeat builds a report for memorytree-workflow, it only reads manifests from that project.

The solution: When buildReport is called during heartbeat, pass the manifest dirs of all OTHER registered projects too. The manifests from other projects will then be included, so the "Projects" page shows all 3 projects.

Key insight from reading the code:
- parseCleanMarkdownMessages(m, root) uses m.repo_clean_path joined with root, OR falls back to m.global_clean_path (absolute path). For cross-project manifests, repo_clean_path won't work (it's relative to the other project's root), but global_clean_path is an absolute path that will work fine.
- resolveRawPath(m, root) similarly: repo_raw_path is relative to root (won't work cross-project), but global_raw_path is absolute (will work).
- transcriptOutputPath(output, m) uses m.repo_clean_path || m.global_clean_path - this is OK.
- The transcript HTML rendering calls parseCleanMarkdownMessages(m, root) which passes the CURRENT project's root. For foreign manifests, m.repo_clean_path would point to a wrong location. But the fallback to m.global_clean_path (absolute) should work.

Actually wait - parseCleanMarkdownMessages does:

const cleanPath = m.repo_clean_path
    ? join(root, m.repo_clean_path)
    : m.global_clean_path

So if m.repo_clean_path exists (it's a relative path like Memory/06_transcripts/clean/...), it will join it with the CURRENT project's root, which is WRONG for foreign project manifests.

For foreign project manifests, we need to use global_clean_path instead. The repo_clean_path only makes sense within the owning project's root.

So the approach needs to be slightly more careful. For manifests from other projects, we need to use their absolute paths.

Options:

Option A: Add extraManifestRoots to BuildReportOptions. In buildReport, load manifests from all roots. For cross-project manifests, when calling parseCleanMarkdownMessages, use global_clean_path instead of trying to join with current root.

The issue: parseCleanMarkdownMessages(m, root) uses root only to resolve repo_clean_path. If we pass the other project's root for those manifests, it works. But we'd need to know which root to use for each manifest.

Option B: Add extraManifestRoots and for each additional root, load manifests AND tag them with their origin root. Then dispatch parseCleanMarkdownMessages with the correct root per manifest.

Actually, looking more carefully:
- global_clean_path is an absolute path. If it's set, we should prefer it over repo_clean_path (which is repo-relative).
- The issue is parseCleanMarkdownMessages prioritizes repo_clean_path over global_clean_path.

The cleanest fix: modify parseCleanMarkdownMessages to accept an optional override root or just use global_clean_path when available as absolute path.

Actually the simplest fix: for foreign manifests (from other projects), their global_clean_path will be valid absolute paths. We can create a helper that loads manifests from multiple roots.

Simplest implementation plan:

1. BuildReportOptions: add extraManifestRoots?: string[]
2. buildReport: after loadManifests(root), also load from each extra root and merge
3. For the merged foreign manifests, when calling parseCleanMarkdownMessages, we need to handle the root correctly. The simplest fix: modify parseCleanMarkdownMessages to accept an optional second root that can be the actual owning root, OR better yet, just make it prefer global_clean_path as an absolute path when repo_clean_path would fail.

Wait, actually let me re-read:

export function parseCleanMarkdownMessages(m: ManifestEntry, root: string): RenderedMessage[] {
  const cleanPath = m.repo_clean_path
    ? join(root, m.repo_clean_path)
    : m.global_clean_path

1→/**
     2→ * Link graph construction: detects [[session_id]] / [[stem]] references
     3→ * in clean markdown content and builds forward/backlink maps.
     4→ */
     5→
     6→import { existsSync, readFileSync } from 'node:fs'
     7→import { basename, join } from 'node:path'
     8→
     9→import type { ManifestEntry } from '../../types/transcript.js'
    10→import type { LinkGraph } from '../../types/report.js'
    11→
    12→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    13→// Link graph builder
    14→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    15→
    16→export function buildLinkGraph(manifests: ManifestEntry[], root: string): LinkGraph {
    17→  const forwardLinks: Record<string, string[]> = {}
    18→  const backlinks: Record<string, string[]> = {}
    19→
    20→  // Build lookup table: various identifiers → canonical session_id
    21→  const lookup: Record<string, string> = {}
    22→  for (const m of manifests) {
    23→    // Register by session_id
    24→    lookup[m.session_id] = m.session_id
    25→    // Register by artifact stem (e.g. "019cf4b1-....__0ebaa458")
    26→    const cleanPath = m.repo_clean_path || m.global_clean_path
    27→    if (cleanPath) {
    28→      const stem = basename(cleanPath, '.md')
    29→      if (stem) lookup[stem] = m.session_id
    30→    }
    31→  }
    32→
    33→  for (const m of manifests) {
    34→    const cleanPath = resolveCleanPath(m, root)
    35→    if (!cleanPath || !existsSync(cleanPath)) continue
    36→
    37→    let content: string
    38→    try {
    39→      content = readFileSync(cleanPath, 'utf-8')
    40→    } catch {
    41→      continue
    42→    }
    43→
    44→    const refs = extractLinks(content)
    45→    for (const ref of refs) {
    46→      const targetId = lookup[ref]
    47→      if (!targetId || targetId === m.session_id) continue // skip self-refs
    48→
    49→      // Forward: m → target (immutable update)
    50→      const fwd = forwardLinks[m.session_id] ?? []
    51→      if (!fwd.includes(targetId)) {
    52→        forwardLinks[m.session_id] = [...fwd, targetId]
    53→      }
    54→
    55→      // Backlink: target ← m (immutable update)
    56→      const back = backlinks[targetId] ?? []
    57→      if (!back.includes(m.session_id)) {
    58→        backlinks[targetId] = [...back, m.session_id]
    59→      }
    60→    }
    61→  }
    62→
    63→  return { backlinks, forwardLinks }
    64→}
    65→
    66→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    67→// Link extraction
    68→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    69→
    70→/** Extract all [[...]] references from text. */
    71→export function extractLinks(content: string): string[] {
    72→  const results: string[] = []
    73→  const re = /\[\[([^\][\n]+)\]\]/g
    74→  let match: RegExpExecArray | null
    75→  while ((match = re.exec(content)) !== null) {
    76→    const ref = match[1]?.trim()
    77→    if (ref && ref.length > 0) {
    78→      results.push(ref)
    79→    }
    80→  }
    81→  return results
    82→}
    83→
    84→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    85→// Path helpers
    86→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

    88→export function resolveCleanPath(m: ManifestEntry, root: string): string | null {
    89→  if (m.repo_clean_path) {
    90→    return join(root, m.repo_clean_path)
    91→  }
    92→  if (m.global_clean_path) {
    93→    return m.global_clean_path
    94→  }
    95→  return null
    96→}

    13→export function computeStats(
    14→  manifests: ManifestEntry[],

    16→): ReportStats {

    42→  const from = dates[0] ?? ''
    43→  const to = dates[dates.length - 1] ?? ''
    44→

    46→    totalSessions,
    47→    totalMessages,
    48→    totalToolEvents,
    49→    activeDays: daySet.size,
    50→    dateRange: { from, to },

    54→    toolCounts,
    55→  }

    58→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    59→// Day buckets: 'YYYY-MM-DD' → session count
    60→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    61→
    62→export function buildDayBuckets(manifests: ManifestEntry[]): Record<string, number> {
    63→  const buckets: Record<string, number> = {}
    64→  for (const m of manifests) {
    65→    const day = isoDay(m.started_at)
    66→    if (day) {
    67→      buckets[day] = (buckets[day] ?? 0) + 1
    68→    }
    69→  }
    70→  return buckets
    71→}
    72→
    73→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    74→// Week buckets: 'YYYY-WNN' → message count
    75→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    76→
    77→export function buildWeekBuckets(manifests: ManifestEntry[]): Record<string, number> {
    78→  const buckets: Record<string, number> = {}
    79→  for (const m of manifests) {
    80→    const week = isoWeek(m.started_at)
    81→    if (week) {
    82→      buckets[week] = (buckets[week] ?? 0) + m.message_count
    83→    }
    84→  }
    85→  return buckets
    86→}

    88→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    89→// Tool name extraction
    90→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

    92→/**
    93→ * Extract tool names from tool event summary strings.
    94→ * Summary format is typically: "function_call input=..." or "Bash ..." etc.
    95→ */
    96→export function extractToolNames(summaries: string[]): string[] {
    97→  return summaries.map(s => {
    98→    const trimmed = s.trim()
    99→    // Try to extract first identifier word
   100→    const match = trimmed.match(/^([A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_:-]*)/)
   101→    if (match?.[1]) {
   102→      return match[1]
   103→    }
   104→    return 'unknown'
   105→  })
   106→}
   107→
   108→/**
   109→ * Accumulate tool name counts into an existing map.
   110→ */
   111→export function accumulateToolCounts(
   112→  toolCounts: Record<string, number>,
   113→  names: string[],
   114→): Record<string, number> {
   115→  const result = { ...toolCounts }
   116→  for (const name of names) {
   117→    result[name] = (result[name] ?? 0) + 1
   118→  }
   119→  return result
   120→}

   122→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   123→// Internal helpers
   124→// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
   125→
   126→/** Extract 'YYYY-MM-DD' from an ISO timestamp. Returns '' if invalid. */
   127→function isoDay(ts: string): string {
   128→  if (!ts) return ''
   129→  const match = ts.match(/^(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2})/)
   130→  return match?.[1] ?? ''
   131→}
   132→
   133→/** Compute 'YYYY-WNN' ISO week string from an ISO timestamp. */
   134→function isoWeek(ts: string): string {
   135→  if (!ts) return ''
   136→  try {
   137→    const d = new Date(ts)
   138→    if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return ''
   139→    return isoWeekKey(d)
   140→  } catch {
   141→    return ''
   142→  }
   143→}
   144→
   145→/**
   146→ * Compute 'YYYY-WNN' ISO week key from a Date object.
   147→ * Exported so chart renderers can reuse without duplicating the formula.
   148→ */
   149→export function isoWeekKey(d: Date): string {
   150→  // ISO week: the week containing Thursday; Monday = week start
   151→  const thursday = new Date(d)
   152→  thursday.setDate(d.getDate() + (4 - ((d.getDay() + 6) % 7 + 1)))
   153→  const year = thursday.getFullYear()
   154→  const jan4 = new Date(year, 0, 4)
   155→  const week = Math.ceil(
   156→    ((thursday.getTime() - jan4.getTime()) / 86400000 + jan4.getDay() + 1) / 7,
   157→  )
   158→  return `${year}-W${String(week).padStart(2, '0')}`
   159→}

<thinking>
Now I have a complete picture of the codebase. Let me design the solution:

Current flow in heartbeat.ts:
1. Loop over projects
2. For each project: processProject(config, projectPath, projectName, entry)
3. Inside processProject: if generateReport, call buildReport({ root: projectPath, output: join(projectPath, 'Memory', '07_reports'), ... })
4. buildReport calls loadManifests(root) which only reads from root/Memory/06_transcripts/manifests/

Solution: Pass extra manifest roots from other projects into buildReport.

The cleanest way:
1. Add extraManifestRoots?: string[] to BuildReportOptions
2. In buildReport, after loadManifests(root), also load manifests from each extraManifestRoot and merge
3. In heartbeat.ts's processProject, pass the other projects' manifest dirs

But wait — there's a problem. The manifests from other projects have repo_clean_path which is relative to their own project root (not the current project's root). When parseCleanMarkdownMessages(m, root) is called with the current project's root, the repo_clean_path will point to the wrong place.

Looking at the code:

export function parseCleanMarkdownMessages(m: ManifestEntry, root: string): RenderedMessage[] {
  const cleanPath = m.repo_clean_path
    ? join(root, m.repo_clean_path)
    : m.global_clean_path

And resolveRawPath:

function resolveRawPath(m: ManifestEntry, root: string): string | null {
  if (m.repo_raw_path) {
    return join(root, m.repo_raw_path)
  }
  if (m.global_raw_path) {
    return m.global_raw_path
  }
  return null
}

So for manifests from OTHER projects, if they have repo_clean_path, they'll be resolved against the wrong root. But they also have global_clean_path which is an absolute path.

Looking at the fallback logic:
- parseCleanMarkdownMessages: if m.repo_clean_path exists AND the file doesn't exist at join(root, m.repo_clean_path), it returns empty. But if m.global_clean_path exists, it will use that as fallback... wait no, it checks m.repo_clean_path first:

const cleanPath = m.repo_clean_path
  ? join(root, m.repo_clean_path)  // will resolve to wrong place for other projects
  : m.global_clean_path

So for other projects' manifests, m.repo_clean_path will be non-empty (e.g., Memory/06_transcripts/clean/claude/2026/03/abc.md) but resolved against the wrong root, so the file won't exist and it'll return [].

BUT wait - for the projects/index.html page (which is what the user wants to fix), the manifests are just grouped by extractProject(m.cwd) - that just reads m.cwd which is already in the manifest as a string. So for the Projects page specifically, we just need the manifests loaded - we don't need to read the actual file content.

For the Dashboard, it uses computeStats(manifests, toolCounts) and renderDashboard(stats, manifests, t) - which only use manifest metadata (session counts, dates, etc.), not file content.

For individual transcript rendering, the parseCleanMarkdownMessages is called, but for other projects' manifests, the repo_clean_path will resolve to a wrong path and the file won't exist, so it'll try global_clean_path which IS the absolute path... wait, no. Let me re-read:

const cleanPath = m.repo_clean_path
  ? join(root, m.repo_clean_path)  // wrong root, file won't exist
  : m.global_clean_path
if (!cleanPath || !existsSync(cleanPath)) return []

It uses repo_clean_path first if it exists, and if the file doesn't exist at that path, it returns []. So transcript content from other projects would be empty.

Similar for resolveRawPath:

if (m.repo_raw_path) {
  return join(root, m.repo_raw_path)  // wrong path
}
if (m.global_raw_path) {
  return m.global_raw_path  // absolute path, correct!
}

For stats: toolCounts is accumulated by reading raw files. For other projects' manifests with repo_raw_path but wrong root, it'll fail silently. But global_raw_path would work.

So the main issue is: for the "global" mode where we include manifests from other projects, we should prefer global_ paths over repo_ paths when they're from a different root.

Better approach: When loading manifests from other projects, we need to know their root so we can resolve paths correctly.

Simplest approach that actually works:

Option A: Add manifestRoots?: string[] to BuildReportOptions - these are additional roots to load manifests from. For manifests loaded from these roots, we need to pass the correct root when resolving paths.

But this requires threading the "correct root" through parseCleanMarkdownMessages, resolveRawPath, etc.

Option B: Since manifests have global_clean_path and global_raw_path as absolute paths, we can add a simple flag: when a manifest doesn't belong to the current root, skip path resolution and only use global paths.

Actually, looking more carefully at parseCleanMarkdownMessages:

export function parseCleanMarkdownMessages(m: ManifestEntry, root: string): RenderedMessage[] {
  const cleanPath = m.repo_clean_path
    ? join(root, m.repo_clean_path)
    : m.global_clean_path
  if (!cleanPath || !existsSync(cleanPath)) return []

If repo_clean_path is set (e.g., Memory/06_transcripts/clean/claude/...), it'll try to join with root which is the wrong project root. The file won't exist. Then it returns [] - empty messages.
